Southwest Civilian Aviation Negotiates Filing Procedures 28

And Negotiates Postal Transport Contract Methods

(Nanjing) Liu Peiquan, the organizer of the Southwest Five Provinces Civilian Aviation's opening of five air routes including Guangzhou to Longzhou, came to Beijing for the second time on the 21st. He immediately went to the Ministry of Communications to meet with Wei Yifu, Director of the Postal Department, to negotiate filing procedures and to establish a postal transport contract. Liu said that the Southwest Five Provinces Civilian Aviation Company has a capital of two million yuan and plans to open five air routes: 1. Guangzhou to Longzhou; 2. Nanning to Guiyang; 3. Guiyang to Kunming; 4. Guangzhou to Qiongzhou and Beihai; 5. Guangzhou to Fujian. It is planned to purchase ten aircraft for use. The company has recently received the required capital, and has been established in Guangzhou. It has ordered two aircraft from the American Stenlin Aircraft Factory. These aircraft passed Shanghai a few days ago en route to Hong Kong, and will be installed within the week. They will then fly to Guangzhou for test flights on the Guangzhou-Longzhou route. Formal service is expected to begin in January of next year. The route is 520 kilometers long. During the trial operation, it has been decided that the itinerary will initially be a one-way flight, with the aircraft flying from Guangzhou one day and returning from Longzhou the next day. Flight stations have been set up in Wuzhou and Nanning to carry passengers and mail. Airport radio and other facilities have been completed. A temporary airport has also been opened in Guiping for emergency use. After the route is successfully operated, more aircraft will be purchased to operate the Nanning-Guiyang route, and then the Kunming, Guangzhou, and Qiongzhou routes. As for the Guangzhou-Fujian route, it will be discontinued because the China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong route already passes through the area. The purpose of this trip to Beijing is to negotiate filing procedures with the Ministry of Communications and to establish a postal transport contract. After these matters are completed in three or four days, he will return to Shanghai and then to Guangzhou to prepare for the opening of service. (Special telegram of the 31st)

Kong Xiangxi Takes Office at the Economic Commission 29

Discusses the Problem of Reorganizing Land Taxes

(Nanjing) The National Government recently appointed Chiang Kai-shek and Kong Xiangxi as Standing Committee Members of the National Economic Council according to the revised organizational regulations. It is learned that Kong took office on the 20th. (Central News Agency telegram of the 21st)

(Nanjing) Kong Xiangxi told a Central News Agency reporter on the morning of the 21st that the plan for reorganizing land taxes is currently under discussion with his subordinates. There are many types of surcharges on land taxes in various provinces, and the tax burden is too heavy, causing great suffering to farmers. Therefore, the first step in reorganizing land taxes is to alleviate the suffering of farmers and strictly reduce various surtaxes. The central government will find ways to compensate local governments for losses incurred due to the reduction of surtaxes. Customs duties and salt taxes are also being reorganized, and the principle is to seek fairness. For example, the revenue from sugar tax has decreased after a slight increase in the tax rate, and this urgently needs to be reorganized. In short, all taxes, whether increased or decreased, should be based on the premise of not harming the people's vitality. (Central News Agency telegram of the 21st)

(Nanjing) Minister of Finance Kong issued a sudden order on the 21st, strictly ordering his subordinates to work diligently for the public good and prohibiting tax collection agencies and collectors from overcharging or embezzling funds. (Central News Agency telegram of the 21st)

Tense European Situation; Britain Holds the Key to War and Peace 30

France and Germany Massively Arming, Extreme Anxiety

Frequent Diplomatic Contacts Among Countries, Resembling Pre-War Conditions

(London) After participating in a debate on foreign affairs in the House of Commons, British Foreign Secretary Simon is scheduled to depart for Paris tomorrow afternoon. He and his wife will stay at the British Embassy in Paris until Saturday. British Prime Minister MacDonald said in the House of Commons today that during the parliamentary recess, British cabinet members did not want to formally tour Europe for disarmament matters. Foreign Secretary Simon will now be traveling to Italy for a Christmas holiday in Pichi. When passing through the capitals of various countries, he may have the opportunity to meet with cabinet members of those countries. It is learned that both Britain and France believe that without resuming the Geneva disarmament conference, there will be no perfect plan. France fears that Britain will make concessions to Germany, so it advocates that those who support the League of Nations should immediately reach a draft disarmament treaty and make Germany responsible for making a choice, so that everyone can see Germany's attitude. According to French sources, Germany has reorganized its domestic war debts. The army has been reorganized, and the national defense force has a total of 265,000 people. In addition, there are 80,000 police officers who have received military training. Military officers are not included in this number. France has an army of 428,000 men, of which 172,000 are volunteers. Furthermore, France's military service period has been shortened to one year, resulting in a reduction in troop strength and a weakening of its war power. France is now planning to befriend Russia, but the majority opinion in Paris is that European peace depends on Britain's clear announcement of its policies. (Reuters telegram of the 21st)

Simon's European Mission 31

To Ascertain the Final Opinions of France, Germany, and Italy

Preliminary Negotiations Will Only Involve Mediation

Declaration to be Issued Today Before Departing for France

(London) The cabinet held its weekly routine meeting, and almost all of the meeting time was devoted to discussing Foreign Secretary Simon's upcoming trip to continental Europe. Regarding this matter, the cabinet adopted an important decision on procedure, namely that Simon would first go to the House of Commons to make a declaration tomorrow morning, and depart for France at 1:45 PM, staying at the British Embassy in Paris. He will then go to Geneva on Saturday, and from there directly to Capri, Italy, to rest. He will meet with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini approximately when he departs to return to the country. At that time, British Ambassador to Germany Phipps will be able to report to him the results of the ambassador's upcoming negotiations with the German Foreign Minister. Simon will then compare Phipps' report with the opinions expressed to him by Peng Gu. In this way, the opinions of both France and Germany can be conveyed to Mussolini simultaneously, and Simon can be sure of the policies Italy will adopt regarding disarmament and the League of Nations. This is the main purpose of Simon's trip to Europe. The general impression is that the cabinet meeting reaffirmed its trust in Simon, allowing him to conduct diplomatic negotiations and bring the preliminary negotiation period to an end. During this preliminary negotiation period, Britain is only engaging in mediation. Simon will return to England on January 7 next year. From this perspective, it can be seen that the British cabinet will ultimately decide what attitude to take only after Simon returns home and reports. That time will be in mid-January next year, when the Disarmament Conference reconvenes. This afternoon, Simon met with French Ambassador to Britain Corbin for a long time. (Havas)

Major Espionage Bust in Paris 34

Branches Established Worldwide

Over Fifty People Have Been Detained

(Paris) Since the arrest of 18 spies here, it has been learned that a large espionage organization of a certain country has been discovered. Among the 18 people arrested are two Russian-American couples and the daughter of a former politician from Paris. It is reported that two Russians who lead the organization have escaped. A large amount of money, a radio engine, and various reactionary documents were seized during the arrest. Documents from various countries are prepared, including Chinese. It is reported that some of them are related to maritime and air defense and commercial espionage. The US State Department has cabled the US Ambassador in Paris to provide accurate information. It is reported that the nationalities of those arrested are extremely mixed, including Italians, Czechs, and Norwegians. The first people arrested were a Polish medical student couple. This large-scale arrest occurred at the same time as the government announced that it would allocate large sums of money to expand defenses along the border to the coastline. Authorities have been investigating this organization for several years, and it has only been cracked down on today. In recent years, French authorities have paid particular attention to espionage activities along the border, as espionage incidents occur frequently. Their greatest goal is to probe the truth about French border forts. After the arrested individuals were uncovered by detectives, they were detained in various detention centers. Those who entered American citizenship were a travel agent from Orange, New York, named Swidge. Two other Englishmen are also suspected of conspiracy, as is a merchant born in Romania named Baykovitz, whose wife, Knoruk, was also arrested. (Reuters telegram of the 20th)

(Paris) Police are actively investigating the recent espionage case. Today, they arrested another ten suspects, including a Romanian naturalized in Canada, named Begovitz, who is the leader of the spies. Begovitz and his accomplices were about to escape when the police arrived. Police seized various documents and a complete set of secret radio transceivers in their residence. Their actions are likely related to the Soviet government. (Havas telegram of the 20th)

(Paris) According to reports, the authorities have discovered an espionage organization and have detained over fifty people to date. The organization has branches throughout Europe or the world. Among those detained is a translator from the Naval Ministry. According to the Petit Parisien, police have seized many documents and a secret radio transmitter in connection with the case. French police officers have flown to Warsaw to investigate events related to the case. Another newspaper reported that the US government has ordered the US Ambassador to France to report the details, as it is said that there is an American couple among those detained. (National Telegram of the 21st)

(Washington) The US State Department expressed surprise after receiving news that two American citizens in Paris had been arrested on charges of privately possessing French military documents and photographs. The State Department's files show that both had obtained proper passports. It is expected that the US Ambassador to France will be instructed to investigate the matter. (National Telegram of the 20th)

Close Cooperation Between France and Russia 35

France Assists Russia in Manufacturing Aircraft

Russia Supplies Kerosene in Exchange

(Changchun) It is reliably learned that when French Air Minister Guot visited Russia, he signed a contract with Soviet Russia, under which France would send 2,000 technicians and workers skilled in manufacturing aircraft to Russia, and Russia would supply kerosene to France in exchange. The technicians departed for Russia from France earlier this month. As a result, France's long-standing shortage of kerosene can be remedied by the Soviet Union, while Soviet Russia, which has traditionally purchased aircraft from France and Italy, can manufacture them domestically. Therefore, the economic cooperation between France and Russia is highly valued. (Dentsu telegram of the 21st)

US Army Adds Large Searchlights

For Nighttime Air Defense

(London) Britain is increasing its air force strength. Future air force budget proposals will include funding for the formation of four new air force squadrons. One of these squadrons will replace the 100th Squadron, which is about to go to Singapore to strengthen the British air force there. The Times reported that the squadron recently acquired torpedo bombers from the Vickers factory, etc. (Reuters telegram of the 21st)

(New York) The US Army has ordered 104 60-inch anti-aircraft lights from the Spey Company. Each light has 800 million candlepower and can be seen from 15,000 feet away in clear weather, allowing indicators to point out aircraft and automatically opening anti-aircraft guns. All of these lights are mobile, and their light can be seen up to 100 miles away, making them the world's largest searchlights. (National Telegram of the 20th)

Avenol Indicates League of Nations Weaknesses Should be Reformed 39

Basic Principles Need Not be Disturbed

Working Methods Can Be Improved

(Paris) The Foreign Affairs Committee of the Chamber of Deputies held a meeting at which League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol reported on how the League of Nations' weaknesses were being criticized. He paid particular attention to (1) the equality of rights of all countries in the League of Nations, (2) the revision of peace treaties, and (3) the link between the League of Nations Covenant and the Treaty of Versailles. Avenol believed that the weaknesses of the League of Nations could be reformed based on the criticisms, without disturbing the basic principles of the League of Nations, because these principles should ultimately be maintained. He believed that the root of the League of Nations' problems lay in its poor working methods. If working methods could be improved, then the criticisms would naturally cease. Avenol concluded that the League of Nations was still needed by the international community and should therefore be allowed to exist. After Avenol spoke, Foreign Affairs Committee Chairman Herriot presented a report on the exchange of views between France and Germany. The committee then expressed the hope that the government would make a clear announcement on the situation of the Franco-German talks and the measures it intended to take before the Chamber of Deputies adjourned. Deputy Flaubert said that it was dangerous for France and Germany to directly negotiate a non-aggression treaty, because the Geneva Declaration of December 11, 1932, did not disregard French security by allowing Germany equality in armaments. Moreover, the four countries of France, Germany, England, and Italy had solemnly declared that the borders of Germany with France and Belgium had been guaranteed by England and Italy. All countries should maintain the status quo on this matter and not raise issues. With these two points in mind, it was inappropriate for France and Germany to conclude another non-aggression treaty. (Note: The two points referred to by Flaubert are, first, the declaration jointly issued by the five countries of England, the United States, France, Germany, and Italy when Germany was allowed to participate in the Disarmament Conference last December, and second, the Locarno Treaty). (Havas telegram of the 20th)

US Naval Reorganization Plan Could be Realized Next Spring 40

Increasing Efficiency and Reducing Expenses

More Opportunities for Naval Academy Graduates

(Washington) Today, the White House spokesman said that the merger of the US Coast Guard and the Navy will likely be realized soon, but the exact date may not be announced until after the new year. Currently, officials from the Coast Guard, the Navy, and the Treasury Department are consulting with the President on the merger plan. It is reported that the US President advocates that the Coast Guard form its own team within the Navy, managed in the same way as the Marine Corps, in the hope of increasing efficiency and saving money. It is rumored that under the current plan, officers within the Coast Guard will be assigned from Naval Academy graduates, and the Coast Guard Academy in New London will be converted into a graduate research institute for Naval Academy graduates, with the aim of further study and saving expenses. In recent years, almost half of Naval Academy graduates have switched to civilian positions, and in the future there will be more opportunities for them. (National News Agency telegram of the 21st)

French Government's Financial Bill Passed Again in Senate 41

Returned to Chamber of Deputies for Second Reading

(Paris) Today, the Senate passed the entire financial bill with 266 votes against 51 votes. The bill has now been returned to the Chamber of Deputies for a second reading. It seems that the passage of the bill by both houses is no longer a problem. Today, the Foreign Affairs Committee discussed the issue of Germany's disarmament proposals and recommended that the government determine its policies before Congress adjourns. (Reuters telegram of the 20th)

(Paris) The Senate continued to discuss the financial bill in the afternoon, during which the clause on taxing agricultural interest aroused a lengthy debate. The result was that it was removed by a majority of 193 votes to 98 votes. The clauses were then passed item by item, and a modification was made to the clause extending the period for granting import licenses, arguing that the order on taxing such licenses should be approved by Congress immediately, rather than applying the deadline for requesting approval set for tariff matters. The reason for this was to indicate that the license tax was a taxation measure, not a tariff issue. This clause was then passed in accordance with the amended text. Budget Minister Marchandeau said that this measure was particularly applicable to new products that could compete with domestic products and could generate unemployment in mining areas. At that point, the Senate passed the entire financial reorganization bill by a majority of 206 votes to 57 votes. Finally, Financial Committee Rapporteur Reynaud said that the Chamber of Deputies' original bill stipulated that the national treasury's income would be 4,788,000,000 francs, while the Senate Financial Committee increased it to 4,938,000,000 francs, and what the Senate passed was only 4,632,000,000 francs, of which (1) saving government expenses accounted for 1,702,000,000 francs, (2) extraordinary income accounted for 1,223,000,000 francs, (3) 500,000,000 francs could be obtained from monitoring tax revenues, and (4) 1,207,000,000 francs could be obtained from reorganizing tax sources. Reynaud concluded that it was still necessary to save government expenses. (Havas telegram of the 20th)

Inauguration of the Oriental Academy at the Pantheon in Rome 42

Sponsored by Founder Dusi and Mussolini

Aims to Promote Cultural and Economic Relations Between Italy and Asia

Rome: The Middle East and Far East Academy was inaugurated this morning at the Pantheon. The ceremony was grand. Under the bronze statue of Caesar Augustus, the names of the academy's founders were engraved, including the current Minister of Education, Ercole, and the academy's president, Santi. Members of the diplomatic corps, representatives from both houses of parliament, and many cabinet members attended in person. Eastern students attending the Asian Students Conference in Rome also participated in the ceremony. President Santi delivered a lengthy speech to the Eastern students. (Havas dispatch of the 21st)

Rome: The Middle East and Far East Academy held its opening ceremony at the Pantheon today. Students from Egypt, India, China, and Japan who came to Rome from various European countries to attend the Asian Students Conference all participated in the ceremony. The original proposer of the Middle East and Far East Academy was Mr. Dusi, a member of the Italian Central Research Institute. Dusi had previously led an Italian scientific expedition to Tibet and Nepal. Later, Mahatma Gandhi visited Rome and supported the idea, leading to the decision to establish the Middle East and Far East Academy. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini was very concerned about this matter and ordered the establishment of the academy on February 16 of this year. Its purpose is to promote cultural relations between Italy and the countries of Central, South, and East Asia and to study the economic issues related to these countries. The former Minister of Education, Santi, serves as the president of the academy. Dusi serves as the vice president in charge of cultural research. Count Volpi, a cabinet member, serves as the vice president in charge of economic research. Baron Liciaretti and Congressman Tessari serve as consultants to the executive department. The above five key figures are selected by the Prime Minister. In addition, thirteen consultants are selected from various enterprises and academies that have common interests with the Far East Academy. They are appointed by the King of Italy upon the Prime Minister's recommendation. The importance of the academy is evident from this. The founders plan to provide scholarships to Asian students studying in Italy so that they can introduce Italian businesses, especially Italian insurance companies, in Eastern countries in the future. In addition, the academy plans to launch a large-scale magazine and organize an Indian art exhibition in the near future. (Havas dispatch of the 21st)

Germany to Sterilize 400,000 People 47

Eugenics Law to Take Effect on January 1st

(Berlin) The German government's "Elimination of Reproductive Function" law is scheduled to take effect on January 1 of next year. Approximately 400,000 people with hereditary diseases, especially the mentally disabled, will be subject to this law. Surgery can only be performed after a special court order. There will be 1,700 such courts throughout Germany, 1,000 of which will be in Prussia. The cost of the surgery will be 14 million marks. Men only need to pay 20 marks and rest for four days after the surgery. Women's surgery is more complicated, costing 50 marks and requiring at least seven days of bed rest to recover. (Havas dispatch of the 20th)

British House of Commons Debates the Position of the British Cotton Industry 48

Most Trade with China Seized by Japan

Government Representative Says Do Not Be Too Pessimistic

Labour Party Motion Amended and Passed

(London) Today, the House of Commons debated the position of the cotton industry. Labour Party members moved a motion criticizing competitive capitalism and advocating the reorganization of the cotton industry under public ownership to implement a comprehensive cotton industry cooperation policy. Conservative Party member Antrobus stated that the colonial market has been reduced by Japanese competition and that a large part of the trade with China has been lost and cannot be recovered. Liberal Party member Payden responded on behalf of the government, saying that there is no need to be too pessimistic about the cotton industry, that Britain's production costs are higher than those of its competitors and should be reduced, and that the British government has been paying close attention to Japanese competition. The House of Commons should not constantly bring it up, as this will not help Lancashire and will not help the relationship between the British and Japanese governments. "We do not have any magic to immediately change the position of the cotton industry. Lancashire can only work hard to innovate and adapt to the times to help itself." Antrobus proposed amending the Labour Party's motion, stating only that the cotton industry intends to improve its organization and that the House of Commons welcomes any methods proposed by the cotton industry that can achieve this goal. This amendment was passed by 135 votes to 30. The debate was thus postponed indefinitely. (Reuters dispatch of the 20th)

Therefore, even if Chinese Eastern Railway employees are Russian, they will be punished according to the law if they violate national laws. U.S. President and Congress Tend to Improve the Position of Silver and Oppose Inflation of Currency 51

Substantive Action Will Be Taken After Congress Convenes

(New York) U.S. Speaker of the House Rayburn and Senator Thomas spoke at an economic club here today, both stating that the President and Congress are against the indiscriminate issuance of banknotes and the inflation of currency, but advocate improving the position of silver. They also said that the President will be able to obtain congressional support to continue reducing the gold dollar to only be worth fifty cents. Thomas, as the leader of the inflation faction in Congress, firmly asserted today that inflation is absolutely inevitable. He believes that substantive action will be taken after Congress convenes on the third of next month, because it is estimated that government spending for the coming year, including relief programs, will total 6 billion yuan, while revenue may only be 3 billion yuan. If the shortfall of half is not made up by reducing the value of the gold dollar, then the government will have to admit bankruptcy. Moreover, the slower the reorganization of the currency system, the lower the value of the gold dollar will be, and the greater the crisis of real inflation will be. Speaker Rayburn expressed agreement with the government's plan and the President's views, saying that we cannot maintain a fixed exchange rate between gold and silver, but we can allow gold and silver to circulate as currency at the same time, without fixing their exchange rate. Rayburn's words show that he does not support setting a fixed exchange rate between gold and silver. It is widely believed here that the U.S. government will also support this view. (National News Agency dispatch of the 20th)

Ancient Handwritten Bible Manuscript 55

British Museum Willing to Pay £100,000

To Buy from the Soviet Government

(London) The British Museum has decided to purchase the oldest and most famous handwritten Bible manuscript, the Codex Sinaiticus, from the Soviet government for a total of £100,000, half of which will be donated by the public and half of which will be allocated by the government. The handwritten manuscript was completed in the middle of the fourth century AD. It was lost for a time, but in 1844 it was rediscovered by the German scholar Tischendorf at St. Catherine's Monastery on Mount Sinai and given to Tsar Alexander II of Russia, where it has been kept in the Royal Library of St. Petersburg ever since. (Havas dispatch of the 21st)

(London) This manuscript is one of the most important ancient notebooks in the world. It was first discovered by the scholar Tischendorf during a trip to St. Catherine's Monastery on Mount Sinai in 1844. When he visited Mount Sinai again in 1853, he discovered most of the notebook. The handwritten manuscript contains most of the Old Testament and is written in Greek. It is treasured by the Russian Emperor. (Reuters dispatch of the 20th)

Astronomical Research Institute Observes Lunar Occultation of Venus and Saturn 82

(Nanjing) The phenomenon of Venus and Saturn being successively occulted by the moon, that is, successively disappearing behind the moon, is quite rare. Astronomers are paying close attention to this phenomenon. The locations where this phenomenon can be observed are primarily in eastern Asia, with Japan being the most convenient. This is because when the phenomenon occurs there, the sun is already near the horizon, making it easier to observe. In our country, the sun is too high in the sky, making observation inconvenient. On that day, staff from the Astronomical Research Institute went to the Zijin Mountain Astronomical Observatory, intending to use the largest reflecting telescope in the Far East to observe this phenomenon. The time Venus disappeared was around 6:21 PM, but due to circuit issues with the equipment, they were unable to observe it. They only saw it reappear around 3:46 PM, appearing slightly below the east-central part of the moon. The crescent moon had a point of light on its eastern edge, visible even to the naked eye, which was Venus. It then gradually moved away, appearing below the moon. At this time, Venus was half dark and half bright, resembling the two phases of the moon, with a luminosity of negative four and an apparent radius of seventeen seconds. Subsequently, they continued to observe the occultation of Saturn. Due to incomplete telescope installation, they only used the attached three-inch telescope for observation. At this time, Saturn's luminosity was only zero point one nine, and its apparent radius was only seven seconds. Furthermore, the sun was still shining brightly in the sky, making it difficult to find. Later, assistant Li Jiancheng saw an elliptical glimmer emerging from the northwest end of the moon's dark edge, disappearing completely at 4:55:37 PM. This elliptical glimmer was Saturn's rings. Afterwards, due to a temporary malfunction in the equipment's circuits, they were unable to observe its reappearance, so they went down the mountain. They observed near the Ming Xiaoling Mausoleum with small binoculars, estimating its reappearance to be around 5:36 PM. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

Public Telegram 99

Telegram from Qingdao to All Newspapers: In recent years, the nation has suffered many misfortunes, and all industries are in decline. Fishermen along the coast have suffered particularly severely, either harassed by bandits or invaded by foreign fishing vessels. Along the thousands of miles of coastline across the country, there is almost no fishing industry to speak of, and the fishermen within these thousands of miles have almost no livelihood to pursue. Our Ministry of Industry, bearing this responsibility, is striving to revive the industry. It has established fisheries management bureaus in coastal provinces such as Guangdong, Fujian, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Hebei, and Shandong, aiming to devise ways to protect fishermen and improve the fishing industry. The laws are well-intentioned and the intentions are good, which is not only a blessing for the fishermen, but also a fortune for the country. We merchants, living by the sea for generations and making a living by fishing, are especially pleased to see this happen. Therefore, upon the arrival of Xu Songpu, the director of the Hebei-Shandong Fisheries Management Bureau, in Qingdao, we immediately met with him and contributed our knowledge to facilitate his work. Xu initially cited the country's difficulties and the Ministry's empty coffers, and then, in the name of the Management Bureau, borrowed money from us to cover operating expenses. Considering the good policies and eagerness to achieve results, we merchants quickly gathered more than 30,000 yuan in cash and lent it to the Fisheries Management Bureau, with Director Xu issuing an official receipt, promising to pay interest at 8 percent per month, and to repay the principal and interest in full by the Ministry of Industry within six months. Our merchants acted righteously, with no other motives mixed into the loan issue, and we did not dare to harbor any mistrust towards this specially established central agency. Who knew that after six months, not a single penny was returned? Director Xu falsely claimed to be going to Beijing and never came back. The Ministry of Industry, under the pretense of this, dismissed Director Xu and appointed Wang Qikun, the section chief of the bureau, as acting director, and then issued a clear order to shut down the office and instructed Acting Director Wang to go to Beijing to finalize the closure. They did not inquire about the debt owed to us merchants. When we merchants submitted a petition to the Ministry requesting payment, the Ministry of Industry claimed that the loan from the Fisheries Bureau had not been reported and that they could not verify and issue it. They instructed us to submit the petition directly to the Bureau. When we merchants followed the order to negotiate with Acting Director Wang, Acting Director Wang pushed the matter away, claiming that it had already been reported to the Ministry. It seems that the Ministry and Bureau are shifting blame and colluding in a scam. Finally, when we merchants telegraphed the Ministry for instructions, they simply ignored us, which is unfathomable to us common people. It was not easy for us poor fishermen from the coast to pool our resources. Once we encounter such an accident, we will be displaced. In addition to still appealing to the Ministry of Industry to return the money, we implore our wise and enlightened officials of the Party and the State, and the enlightened people of the country, to understand our heartfelt feelings and grant us assistance, so that our money can be returned to its original owners and we can safely fish. We are infinitely grateful. Signed, Zhu Yingfu et al., thirty-two coastal fishermen merchants, creditors of the Hebei-Shandong Maritime Fisheries Management Bureau.

Replacement of Guangdong and Hunan Troops in Southern Jiangxi 100

Western Route Army Stationed in the Upper Reaches of the Gan River

Nanchang Correspondence: Since the Fujian Incident occurred, the Guangdong troops suppressing bandits in southern Jiangxi have been withdrawn to guard the northeast of the two rivers. The defense areas north of Ganzhou and west of the Gan River, including Chongyi and Youzhen, have been handed over to the Hunan troops. However, the Nanchang Headquarters did not receive a report when Liangfu Shadi Youzhen and other places were evacuated. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek telegraphed Nanan on the 15th to inquire about the details from Yu Hanmou. At the same time, he ordered a certain unit of the Western Route Army to quickly move in. However, during this troop replacement, local communists took the opportunity to become active. For example, small groups in various places in Yudu changed the flags and numbers of the Fujian Provincial People's Government, extensively proclaiming that there were a lot of salt and kerosene being transported to the red zone for supply, and claiming to attack a certain place or city. Therefore, people could not help but panic. Recently, the Provincial Party Headquarters received news from Ganzhou that, due to the Fujian Incident, the people of Ganzhou were speculating about the movement of the Guangdong troops, resulting in many rumors in the market. In order to stabilize people's hearts, Yu Hanmou, commander of the First Army, telegraphed Li Zhenqiu, commander of the First Division, to instruct Commissioner Zhang to inform the people not to panic each other. The army will set up a city defense command when necessary to maintain law and order. Ganzhou was attacked and destroyed by Peng Dehuai in 1931. After the arduous repairs of the fortifications and various works by the garrison troops, it is quite strong. Now, the Li Division believes that defense is important and has decided to set up a city defense commander to focus on defense. (December 9th)

Guangdong and Guangxi Jointly Suppress Border Bandits 101

Guangdong Mobilizes Garrison Brigade to Increase Defense in the West River

Guangxi Cangwu County Bans All Boats

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Huang San Zha bandit gang on the border between Guangdong and Guangxi is gathering in Jinkeng and other places in the Dongping District of Bobai County, Guangxi Province. The area is adjacent to Hepu County in Guangdong Province, so the bandits often appear in Hepu. The defense forces of the two Guangdongs have repeatedly sent teams to encircle and suppress them, but they have not been able to eliminate the bandits. At the beginning of the month, Luo Ying, the garrison of Hepu, joined the people of the Republic of China and crossed the border into Guangxi to encircle the bandits in Jinkeng. At that time, the people of Dongping District of Guangxi Province also organized a team to assist in the suppression. As a result, many bandits were annihilated in Mazizhang. Four bandits were captured and eight heads of cattle were recovered. During this battle, the Guangdong and Guangxi militias encircled and suppressed the bandits for three days and nights. Several officers and soldiers were injured. The remaining bandits fled into the Longtan Mountains in Dongping. In order to prevent the remaining bandits from resurfacing and consolidate the winter defense, the Guangdong and Guangxi authorities recently urgently needed to dispatch troops to trấn in the West River basin. Guangdong Province recently telegraphed the entire garrison brigade stationed in Qiongya to the West River. The advance troops of the first regiment of the brigade, led by Huang Guoliang, arrived in the province from Haikou on the Hai Diao warship on the 9th of this month. They gathered in Huangpu on the 11th. The next day, the second battalion of the Huang Regiment, led by Mo Fuyi, arrived in Sanshui County in the West River. The remaining first and third battalions departed from Haikou on the 14th and will successively go to Sanshui and Southwest to defend. Two years ago, the garrison brigade was transferred to Qiong. It consisted of three regiments. The second regiment, led by Liu Binggang, had been transferred to the province and stationed at Jiangcun Station in Fucheng. The third regiment, led by Peng Zhifang, will depart from Haikou after Huang Guoliang completes the transport. The first regiment will be stationed in Fengchuan Deqing and the upper reaches of the West River, one regiment will be stationed in Zhaoqing, and one regiment will remain in Sanshui County. The original Independent Fourth Regiment, led by Wang Dinghua, will be transferred from the West River to Haikou to take over the defense of Qiongya. The second battalion of the Wang Regiment, led by He Zhongfan, arrived in Haikou on the 8th, and the first battalion also arrived in Qiongya on the 12th. The third battalion will be transferred to Qinxian to defend. It is expected that they will complete the handover by the end of the month. Guangdong Province has increased the garrison of a guard brigade in the West River. In addition to a part of the army being sent to Rongwei, Teng County, and other places to handle pacification, Guangxi Province has also designated Wuzhou as a water transportation hub. Recently, winter defense has been carried out. Therefore, Cangwu County promulgated temporary measures to ban boats to prevent villains from hiding. The main points of the boat ban measures include: all boats in Anping, Rongcheng, and Xiande Districts in Wuzhou County shall be investigated, numbered, and registered according to the household survey method. The time for boats to depart is set at 6:00 AM every day, and the time for temporary stops is set at 7:00 PM. The district chiefs of each district will convene a meeting to designate a location for boats to gather and anchor, and they are not allowed to anchor freely. Boats are not allowed to travel at night to transport goods or people, to prevent stowaways. If there is a legitimate special emergency and they need to travel at night, they must obtain a special travel permit. If there are other boats from other towns and ports that come to stay, the rural kapitans of the boat owners in that garrison must report to the local public office or village head for verification and examination. (December 15th)

Inspection Record of Jiawang Mining Area 102

The Sunken Area is Approximately Over Two Qing

Compensation for Damaged Farmland is Expected

Xuzhou Correspondence: The sunken farmland near the Jiawang mining area and the dispute between the people and the mine have lasted for many days. The rumors from all sides are inconsistent. In order to clarify the truth, the reporter took the Jinpu No. 8 train to Liuquan at 7:00 AM on the 19th, and then took the Jialiu small train to Jiawang. He immediately went to the sunken farmland to conduct on-site inspections, visited farmers' representatives in Daquan Village, visited the mining authorities of the Jiawang Mine, and visited the coal mine. He took the Jinpu No. 7 train back to Xu at 7:00 PM in the evening. The eyewitness investigation is recorded as follows:

▲Inspection of the Sunken Land: He boarded the train north at about 7:00 AM and arrived at Liuquan in about an hour. Liuquan market is located northeast of the station and belongs to the second district of Tongshan. There are hundreds of households in the market, including the district office, Liuquan Elementary School, and the county-run Agricultural Education Center. The market is still developing. The Jialiu small railway runs east between the market and the station. The track is very narrow. He boarded the small train and went east, passing through the Chaifang and Qingshanquan stations to reach Jiawang. This type of train is dedicated to transporting coal. The coal is produced in Jiawang and transported to Liuquan, and then transferred to various places for sale via the Jinpu Railway. The train runs back and forth five or six times a day. The nearby people can ride the coal trucks at will, which is quite convenient. After getting off the train, he walked northeast from the Jiawang Mine and conducted an on-site inspection in the open field. The sunken land can be found everywhere from Xinqiao in the northeast to Daquan in the southwest. Some of them are evenly sunken, forming a low-lying shape, while others suddenly fall, forming a ground cave. There are also graves that have fallen down. However, according to the trend, the sinking should have occurred in the summer and autumn. Today, except for a few ground caves near Liulin, the rest are planted with two crops of wheat, leaving only the high and low shapes. The Liulin ground cave is about a few feet deep, and in the fourth section of the land south of the mine, there are newly discovered cracks, dozens of them vertically and horizontally. These cracks are about two inches wide and form a curved arc, which is a sign of sinking. Further south, in the land in Xiaohuizi, there are also graves and monuments sinking down. However, the coal-mining layer is several feet below the ground, and it is impossible to sink suddenly to form a precipice. Therefore, they all show a continuous sinking shape, and the tightness of the geology is different, and the degree of emptiness is also different. It is impossible to sink in the same way. Therefore, it is difficult to sink or not sink in the same area, and it presents an uneven state.

▲Talking with Farmers: In the sunken area, they met several farmers and guided them to visit Liu Haiqiu, the village chief of Daquan, and rural leaders Ding Peifan, He Qisheng, Zhu Maogui, and Zhao Xuecheng. According to them, the farmland in the fifth village of the ninth district of Daquan, which belongs to Tengyi, Shandong, has been sinking since this summer, and is still sinking. At that time, the farmers gathered and negotiated with the mine. In September, Cui Gongfu, the magistrate of Teng County, sent a committee member, Liu Qinfang, to come here to assist the mine manager of the mine, Jiang Shanshou, the director of the general affairs office, Sun Fangkai, the engineer Xu En, and the chief of the ninth district, Wang Zhuxi, and representatives of the local village chiefs to stipulate that each acre of sunken land would be compensated with four yuan to compensate for one year's harvest. This compensation would be stored in the Huadong Company for one year, and one year's worth of compensation would be paid. If the grave was sunken, it would be compensated with fifty yuan for relocation. After the joint measurement, about two qing of land in this village were sunken, and about 200 graves were sunken. There were also losses from the southwest to Xiaohuizi Dagouya, but the land belonged to Dagou Village in the second district of Tongshan, so the village could not understand. Among the households in the village that were affected by the disaster were Zhu Maomin, Liu Yupei, Wang Chaogang, Liu Yuxiu, Guo Guangsheng, Lu Shengji, Liu Yulan, Wang Tinggen, Guo Chuansheng, Guo Fengyue, Guo Fengming, Sun the lame, Wang the bald, and Guo the mute, about a hundred households. In addition to the sunken land, the Jialiu Road blocked water and flooded farmland, about 200 steps wide from east to west. At that time, it was also agreed that each acre would be compensated at a price of three and a half yuan. The mine also has new wells that have been excavated but not yet mined, and it is draining water to the outside, flowing southwest to Xiaohuizi, damaging farmland. After negotiation, the mine is responsible for managing the river. The negotiations have been resolved so far, but because the continued measurement has not been cleared, the payment has not been paid. On that day, the farmers there were holding a meeting in the village office to discuss the collection of money.

▲Mine Visit: He then left Daquan and went to the Jiawang Mine to visit the mine manager, Jiang Shanshou. Jiang had gone to Shanghai two days ago, and was received by Sun Fangkai, the director of the general affairs office. According to him, the Jiawang Company was mined in the Qing Dynasty and managed by Yuan Shikai. In 1928, it was handled by Yuanji. In 1930, it was taken over by Huadong Company. Jiawang contributed 800,000 yuan in old products as shares, and Huadong contributed 800,000 yuan in shares, totaling 1.6 million yuan. Wells No. 1, 2, and 3 were opened by Jiawang, and Wells No. 4, 5, 6, and 7 were opened by Yuanji. The company is opening new wells, which have not yet been completed. The forecast is that it will take another year to complete the new wells. At this time, the only way to save the situation is to limit the amount of coal produced on one hand and shorten the completion of the new wells on the other. Currently, Wells No. 4, 5, 6, and 7 produce about 400 to 500 tons of coal per day. The workers are paid on a contract basis, divided into large and small workers. Large workers are paid 50 to 60 cents a day, and small workers are paid 30 to 40 cents a day. They are all poor people working nearby, or farmers doing it in the slack season. As for the negotiations on the sunken land and flooding, the farmers insist that the coal mines in the stratum where the land was not purchased when mining is the reason. According to the Mining Law, mining land only needs to be approved by the official department and notified to the landowner before it can be used. If there is damage, they are only responsible for compensation. Therefore, there is a compensation method that was agreed upon a month ago. It is also an unavoidable fact that water is discharged from the mine. Although the company is responsible for managing the river, it still needs to apply to the official department for approval. Currently, the mining areas that the company has obtained are Jiawang, Dagouyan, Zhuangzhuang, Xiaqiao, Shishanzi, Chaocheng, and Qingshanquan. The company will continue to handle them. However, in recent years, transportation has been slow and sales have been weak. Development and prosperity still depend on the assistance of the government and all parties.

▲Coal Mine Visit: Later, Tan Huanda, a mining engineer, led the inspection of Wells No. 6 and 7. The well is located less than one from the southeast of the main mine. When they arrived at the well, the workers on the well were extracting coal from the well. A steel beam was suspended high above the wellhead, tied with a giant rope. Four ropes struck an iron plate. There were also many small iron cars. The iron plate carried the car down the well, filled with coal, and hoisted it up. Then, a turning machine was used to push the coal into a coal car and transport it to the mine. Tan said that the well is about 12 zhang deep and has a layer of coal. However, the coal here is mixed with stone, which is the so-called coal stone. After mining, the stone and coal are mixed together, with few debris, which is inconvenient to pick. Therefore, the firepower of the coal here is lower, but the price is also lower. It is hoped that the coal in the new wells will be rich in coal seams, so that the company can develop. The workers in the well work eight hours a day. After leaving the well, there is a bathhouse for washing. The excavation site in the well is framed with wooden beams in the shape of a well to prevent the collapse of the stratum. The collapse marks seen outside may be due to the rotting of the abandoned well beams, resulting in a partial collapse, which cannot be collapsed immediately. It was already around 4 o'clock. The reporter did not have time to enter the well, so he took the small train back to Liu and took the Jinpu train back to Xu. (December 20th)

Hangzhou Jiangshan Railway Scheduled to Hold Inauguration Ceremony 103

The inauguration ceremony of the Hangzhou Jiangshan Railway is scheduled to be held on December 28. The bureau has stipulated that all guests should gather at the railway station of Sanlangmiao at 7:00 AM on the morning of that day, take a ferry to the Xixingjiangbian Station, and receive a commemorative badge for the opening of the entire line at the reception office of the station. The badge features a portrait of Mr. Zhang Jingjiang, the founder of the railway, on one side, and a locomotive first invented by Stephenson on the other. The form is very beautiful. The special train is scheduled to depart from Jiangbian Station at 8:00 AM. The bureau has also prepared a variety of exquisite publications, one of which is a record of the bureau's engineering, detailing the organization and evolution of the railway, as well as the engineering design and construction process. The book has about 200 pages, and there are also about 100 design drawings and engineering photographs. The content is very valuable. The second is the bureau's opening commemorative publication, recording the transportation, affairs, machinery, accounting, and general affairs of the railway. It is also very detailed. The third is a detailed record of the scenery of eastern Zhejiang, recording the scenic spots along the railway line. This book is carefully edited by writers Yu Dafu, Fu Donghua, Cheng Wanli, and others. The photos were also taken by famous photographer Lang Jingshan. The content is very exquisite. The fourth is the voucher, and the fifth is the postcard. The printing is exceptionally excellent and beautiful. The above publications will be distributed to the guests for reference and commemoration. Western-style breakfast is also available on the train. The train will arrive in Jinhua in about five hours. Lunch will be served at Jinhua Station. After a short break, the opening ceremony will be held at 2:00 PM. The order of the ceremony is as follows: (1) All stand in silence, (2) Sing the Party song, (3) Bow three times to the Party and National flag and the portrait of the Prime Minister, (4) The chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will, (5) Three minutes of silence, (6) The chairman delivers the opening speech, (7) The director reports, (8) The chief delivers the instructions, (9) The guests speak, (10) Photography. After the opening ceremony, the bureau has pre-arranged for famous bullfights from nearby villages and towns to hold bullfighting shows to add to the fun. Guests who do not go to Yushan will return to Hangzhou on a special train that night. Those who go to Yushan will take a train from Jinhua Station at 7:00 AM the next day (29th) to visit along the line. They will still return to Jinhua on the same day. They will take an early train back to Hangzhou on the 30th. There are sufficient troops and police to maintain order in all the places the road passes through, and the market is extremely stable. There are no security problems along the way.

Teacher Sentenced to Two and a Half Years for Joining the Communist Party 106

Wang Zhu-ming, a 24-year-old teacher at Shanghai Quanzhang Middle School from Jiangning, joined the China Territorial Security League, a communist organization, in May of this year. In July, a secret agent from the Central Party Department stationed in Shanghai reported to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau. He was arrested and sent to the Suzhou High Court. Yesterday (the 21st), Hu Shantong, the presiding judge of the Third Criminal Court, opened the trial. Considering that the defendant was a young student who had gone astray, the circumstances were examined and found to be worthy of leniency. A lighter sentence should be imposed to show compassion. Therefore, the verdict was written as follows: The defendant, with the purpose of endangering the Republic of China, organized a group and was sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment, ordered to be sent to the Reformatory for reflection.

Manufacturer of Poison Pills Escorted to Province 108

On the 14th of this month, the County Public Security Bureau's Inspectorate discovered a poison pill manufacturing facility at No. 114 Changkang Lane on the road. Changzhou

Robbers Shoot and Kill Landlord 110

The house of Zhang Yao-xi, a farmer in Anning Township, the sixteenth district of Wu County, was suddenly attacked by more than a dozen robbers the night before. They knocked on the back door, and Zhang Yao-xi woke up in his dream and immediately called his wife, children, daughters-in-law, etc., to use hoe handles to prop up the back door. The robbers could not open the door, so they shot at the door with guns. Yao-xi's wife, Dai, who was over fifty years old, was shot and killed. The rest of his children and daughters-in-law were also shot and injured. Afterwards, Xie Ying-zheng, the district chief of the sixteenth district, reported to the County Court to send someone for an autopsy. On the morning of the 20th, Prosecutor Guan Jun-jie led officials to the countryside for an autopsy. It was confirmed that Zhang's wife had been shot twice, one bullet entering the chest and exiting the back, and the other entering the waist and exiting the leg. It was determined that she died from gunshot wounds, and the family was instructed to prepare a coffin for burial.

Finance Department Orders Investigation of Education Bureau's Excessive Levies 111

The Finance Department has received an order from the provincial government to substantially reduce and exempt various excessive and miscellaneous levies in each county to relieve the suffering of the people. However, upon investigating the tax schedule submitted by Cheng County, it was discovered that there was an item called "Zhongzi Donation," which was levied at a rate of 3 yuan or 2 yuan per 100 yuan of contract price, depending on whether it was a sandy township or a canal township. Moreover, it was not collected by the county but directly by the Education Bureau. Since the Education Bureau is not a tax collection agency, how can it directly collect taxes? It is said that this "Zhongzi Donation" was approved in October of the tenth year. What authority approved it? What is the method of collection? Are there any regulations? County Magistrate Ruan was specially ordered to investigate and report separately for verification.

Yangzhou

Villagers Surround Gao Gang Survey Committee 114

The Gao Gang area, which belongs to Yangqiao Township in the fifth district of Jiangdu, was originally a commercial port on the Dijie Continent in that township. Now, Wu Rui-bo and others from the seventh district of Taixing have petitioned the provincial department, claiming that although the port is under the jurisdiction of Jiangdu, it is located within the borders of Taixing County and requested that the port be transferred to Taixing. The department ordered the Eighth and Ninth District Commissioner's Offices and the Taixing County Government to dispatch personnel to conduct a joint survey. The residents near the port gathered more than a thousand people and surrounded the committee members, claiming that Gao Gang is part of the Dijie Continent belonging to Yangqiao Township and that there are grain warrants for the entire Dijie Continent as proof, and that there is a natural temple port as the boundary. Administrative matters are all under the jurisdiction of Jiangdu. The port is not an "embedded flower." The temporary defense corps of the port managed to break the siege, and the committee members declared that they would conduct a fair survey. The crowd then dispersed.

At the Huaiyin Chengnan Park Public Theater, during a performance of the "Mandarin Duck Bridge" scene on the 17th, at around 5:00 PM, a martial arts actor named Wei Yan-heng, known as "Nine-Year-Old Red" in the daily theater advertisements, was performing a scene of killing on the bridge. After arriving at the hospital, emergency injections of cardiac stimulants and various surgical procedures were performed. After an entire night, he finally regained consciousness slightly. Fujian Army Invades Zhejiang, Three Routes of Advance 124

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the prelude to the great war of the Fujian army's invasion of Zhejiang has begun. According to news from this port yesterday morning, Jiang Guang-nai and Cai Ting-kai, after the general mobilization order, held a secret meeting of senior cadres with Chen Ming-shu and Dai Ji, with representatives of the Communist army attending. It was decided to attack Zhejiang in three routes, namely: (1) From northern Fujian, through Yanping, via the Xianxia Ridge to Changshan; (2) From Pingnan and Shouning to Xixi, invading Taishun; (3) From Xiapu and Fuding, crossing the Fen Shui Ridge to Pingyang. Currently, all three routes are advancing. According to an aerial reconnaissance report by central planes on the 18th, the main force of the Fujian army concentrated in Gutian is heading towards Pingnan, and the troops in Pingnan are advancing towards Shouning. The front line of Shouning has indeed reached Taishun in Zhejiang. The Fujian army on the Zhenghe southern route is also moving north. Furthermore, the secret meeting decided, based on the offensive and defensive alliance with the Red Army, to organize a front-line committee in the northern Fujian war zone, with Red bandit leaders Zhang Wen-tian and Mao Zedong's younger brother Mao Ze-tan participating in the committee to jointly preside over everything. The front-line committee has great power, in addition to commanding the various troops in combat, it also has the power to handle all political affairs in the war zone. In recent days, the central army in Jiangxi has been suppressing the Red bandits, gaining unprecedented victories. The defeated troops of the bandits have all fled to Fujian. To provide practical assistance to the pseudo-People's Revolutionary Army's invasion to the north, the bandit side is now actively organizing guerrilla units in Lanxi, Yongkang, Wenzhou, Ruian, and other places in Zhejiang, attempting to disrupt the rear of the central army.

This Month's Bonds to Pay Principal and Interest Early 125

Payment on the 30th

In the banking community, the 31st of this month was originally the date for various bonds to begin repaying principal and interest. However, that day falls on a Sunday, and January 1st, 2nd, and 3rd of the 23rd year are New Year's Day. The Central, China, and Transportation Banks, which pay the bonds, will all be closed as usual. It is heard that these banks, in order to safeguard the interests of bondholders, have agreed with the Ministry of Finance to pay the principal and interest of various bonds one day early, on the 30th of this month, for convenience.

All Passengers of the Yuji Shipwrecked Transported by Jiangyuan Warship Yesterday 126

The ship's hull has not yet sunk, and rescue workers have already gone to the scene

The Yuji ship of the Yu Da Company ran aground in the waters off Wenzhou. The passengers were rescued and transported in full by the Jiangyuan warship yesterday. Because the damage to the ship's hull was significant and the situation was dangerous, Lianbao and Yu Da have jointly dispatched the Sanjiang ship and hired engineers and workers to go to the scene for rescue. The details are as follows:

Notification by Japanese warship telegram: After the Yuji ship ran aground, the bow sank into the water. The ship's hull was affected by the first two cabins and has tilted, the situation is precarious. The ship's wireless radio has also been damaged and cannot communicate. The company has repeatedly telegraphed but received no response. It was not until 6:00 PM on the 20th that the Japanese Navy's 27th Destroyer Division, the Hishi, returned to Shanghai from Magong. Because there were Japanese crew members on board the Yuji, it stopped to assist. The shipowner, Abe Totaro, requested the ship to send a wireless telegram to Shanghai, stating that the first two cabins of the Yuji were still submerged in seawater and requesting Shanghai to send a rescue ship to the scene as soon as possible for rescue work. The Jiangyuan warship set sail that evening.

Discuss dispatching technicians and workers: The company received this telegram and immediately informed Lianbao Insurance Company. Because the telegram indicated that the repairs could be completed within a week if assistance was provided, Yu Da and Lianbao consulted with the Hongchang Machinery Factory, hired an engineer, a diver, four carpenters, and twelve workers, brought a large number of materials, and rented a water pump from Yesong to transport them to the scene of the accident to carry out the rescue. Lianbao paid 1,000 yuan in expenses. The workers all boarded the Daxon Company's Sanjiang ship, which departed from Shanghai at 5:00 PM yesterday afternoon. It is expected to arrive in the waters off Wenzhou this afternoon. The ship carried a lot of food for the crew to eat.

Passengers rescued to Shanghai: A total of 154 passengers from the ship, rescued by the Jiangyuan warship and transported to Shanghai, entered the port at around 3:00 PM yesterday and arrived at Gaochang Temple at 4:35 PM. A total of 75 passengers and 79 students from Chen Camp of the Mawei Navy also took the Yuji ship to Shanghai and were transported to Shanghai by the Jiangyuan warship. In addition, a second comprador of the Yuji also came to Shanghai on the Jiangyuan. When the warship arrived at the pier, the naval authorities sent soldiers to take care of them. After the students of the naval training camp landed, they temporarily resided in Gaochang Temple. It is said that they will go to Beijing in a few days. The passengers who arrived in Shanghai dispersed on their own. The soldiers and passengers brought about 100 pieces of luggage. The second comprador of the Yuji went to the company on Yongan Street to report the details of the shipwreck.

Passenger accounts: A passenger told the reporter that the Yuji accident occurred on the night of the 17th. At that time, all the passengers were asleep. They woke up when they heard the alarm. When they went out of the cabin to see, the first two cabins had already flooded. It was not until the morning of the 18th that the French postal ship Rosso arrived to rescue them and send a telegram to the Naval Department. It was not until 5:00 PM that the Jiangyuan and Chuguan arrived. We were able to transfer to the Jiangyuan warship. Because the transfer took time and we encountered wind and waves, we did not depart until yesterday afternoon and arrived in Shanghai today. No passengers were injured in this Yuji accident, and all the luggage and belongings were taken out. However, the cargo inside the ship was completely lost.

Crew members temporarily go to the lighthouse: According to the second comprador of the Yuji who reported to the company, the first and second cabins of the ship were cracked. Fortunately, the engine room and the stern of the ship were intact, so it would not sink immediately. All the crew members inside the ship, because the food had run out, the sailors, firemen, and crew members, about fifty people, are now on the Donggua Mountain lighthouse, waiting for the Shanghai rescue ship to transport food to rescue them. The Yuji ship's hull will not be sacrificed and can be rescued.

Warships protect the work: The company and Lianbao Insurance Company have dispatched a rescue ship and workers, prepared for a week, to repair the holes in the bottom of the ship and help with pumping water. Therefore, the Chuguan dispatched by the Navy is still stationed there for protection. The Japanese Navy's 27th Destroyer Division, the Hishi, is also staying at Donggua Mountain at the request of the shipowner, Abe. The Chuguan ship also sent many sailors to Donggua Mountain to protect the crew. According to the company, whether the Yuji can escape the disaster will depend on the true news after the Sanjiang arrives.

After the Arrest of Jin Xi, the Municipal Government Protests to the Japanese Consul-General, Who Has Already Replied 127

Simple wording stating that Jin's entry into Chinese nationality was not recognized

Jin is still detained in the Japanese police station and has been interrogated several times

The case of Jin Xi, a Korean who had acquired Chinese nationality, being arrested in the French Concession by the Central Police Station of the French Concession with the assistance of the Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai has already attracted attention from all circles. The municipal government authorities also believe that Jin Xi has acquired Chinese nationality, so they have already lodged a protest with the Japanese Consulate-General the other day. According to news from the municipal government yesterday morning, the Japanese Consulate-General's reply has already arrived at the city hall. The details are recorded as follows:

Japanese Consulate Has Already Replied 128

Yesterday morning, reporters from various newspaper agencies specially visited Yu Hong-jun, the Secretary-General of the municipal government, at the city hall for this matter. Mr. Yu was busy with official duties and sent Secretary Huang Shao-zhai to meet them on his behalf. According to the reply, the municipal government, since Jin Xi was arrested in the French Concession and transferred to the Japanese consulate, immediately ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate Jin Xi's nationality and other issues. Based on the results of the investigation, a serious protest was lodged with the Japanese Consulate-General. After many days, the Japanese Consulate-General's reply has already arrived at the city hall. The wording is very simple, only elaborating on the issue of Jin Xi's entry into Chinese nationality. It is claimed that the Japanese government has not recognized Jin Xi's entry into Chinese nationality. In other words, Jin Xi's entry into Chinese nationality has not been approved by the Japanese government.

Public Letter from the Lawyers Association 129

The Shanghai Lawyers Association yesterday sent a public letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government, which stated: We are writing to inform you that our members Lou Yun-mei, Xu Jie, and others have sent a letter stating that they have been entrusted by the family of Jin Xi to negotiate the case of Jin Xi being illegally arrested by the French Central Police Station with the assistance of the Japanese Consulate (already reported in the previous newspaper). After investigation, Jin Xi, a Korean who has acquired Chinese nationality, has already obtained the nationality of the Republic of China, so the Japanese Consulate should not privately arrest him and disregard national sovereignty. The authorities of the French Concession, after assisting the Japanese Consulate in arresting Jin Xi, did not hand him over to the court for trial and judgment, but directly transferred him to the Japanese Consulate, which is deliberately undermining the agreement on the establishment of Chinese courts in the concession. It is their undeniable responsibility. The matter concerns national sovereignty and legal rights. Correspondingly, we request your government to continue protesting to the Japanese Consulate and the authorities of the French Concession, to achieve the goal of returning him to China and safeguarding national sovereignty. We are truly committed to public friendship. To the Shanghai Municipal Government, Shanghai Lawyers Association Standing Committee, 22, 12, 21.

Japanese Side Expresses Opinion on Jin 130

According to a Central News Agency reporter who inquired at the Japanese Consulate-General, the consulate staff said that according to Japanese nationality regulations, any Korean who acquires any nationality is still regarded as Korean by the Japanese government. Because Koreans cannot have dual nationality, Jin Xi, who has acquired Chinese nationality, is still regarded as Korean. However, according to Zhang Ting-rong, director of the information office of the municipal government, the Japanese nationality regulations can only be applied within Japan. Jin Xi's arrest was in Chinese territory. This kind of explanation is obviously a sophistry.

Jin is Still Detained in the Japanese Police Station 131

Since Jin Xi was arrested in the French Concession and transferred to the Japanese Consulate-General in Shanghai, it has been many days. He is currently still detained in the Japanese Consulate Police Station and has been interrogated several times. He will not be transferred to Tokyo in the coming days.

Municipal Government Notifies Various Foreign Embassies of Relocation 132

An office will be established at the original site of Fenglin Bridge

The new building of the municipal government has been fully completed. Various bureaus will move in to work in succession starting from the 25th of this month. The Finance, Public Works, and Public Security Bureaus will postpone the relocation. The municipal government authorities have notified various foreign embassies and consulates of the relocation. Suma to Depart for Fujian Today 133

According to the New Sound Society, Suma Yakichiro, the information department head of the Japanese legation, has received instructions from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to be transferred to the position of Consul-General in Nanjing. As he needs to listen to instructions from Uchida and Shigemitsu regarding the recent diplomatic policy towards China, and to report on the current political situation in China, it was decided that he would first return to Tokyo. He originally planned to take a connecting ship directly from Shanghai back to Japan, but later, due to the urgent need to understand the true situation in Fujian, he temporarily changed his itinerary and is scheduled to take the Jardine Matheson & Co.'s "Jiesheng" ship to Fujian today (the 22nd). He will visit the responsible authorities of the so-called People's Government. This is because when Suma was previously the Consul-General in Guangzhou, Chen Mingshu was the Chairman of Guangdong Province, and Suma had a very deep friendship with Chen. There are rumors that Fujian and Japan have a secret understanding, and that Fujian has a large Japanese sugar loan from Japan. However, the Japanese legation in this city has been making every effort to deny this. Yesterday morning, they even released a telegram from the Consul-General in Fuzhou, Moriya, to reporters, stating that the consumption of white sugar in Fujian Province is extremely low, and even if there is such a loan, it would be fundamentally impossible to redeem it for cash, proving it is not factual. Counselor Ota also solemnly denied it to reporters. He had previously tacitly acknowledged the matter to others. However, based on the observation of the situation, the Japanese side has always attached importance to the Fujian Incident. Given Suma's position and his relationships, this trip is definitely not a simple inspection, but must have considerable political significance. Furthermore, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs has already appointed Counselor Kawasaka Tatsuo of the legation to succeed Suma in his original position as head of the legation's information department. Kawasaka previously served as the head of the information department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the head of the Foreign Affairs Division of the Kwantung Government. He is also extremely familiar with Chinese affairs. He recently traveled to various provinces in South China and returned to Shanghai from Guangdong yesterday morning. Minister Arima, in view of the tense situation in China and the importance of intelligence work, ordered him to take over Suma's former position immediately.

City-Wide Cleaning Campaign to be Held in This City 134

From the 25th to the 31st of this Month

The Municipal Health Bureau, as the end of the year approaches, will, as usual, launch a large-scale cleaning campaign from the 25th of this month. Furthermore, in view of the fact that in the past, shops and households in various streets and alleys arbitrarily dumped garbage, which was detrimental to hygiene, new methods for dumping garbage have been formulated in the jurisdiction of the Second District, Second Precinct of the Public Security Bureau for trial implementation. If successful, they will be extended to the entire city. The details are recorded below.

Designated Week for Campaign 135

The cleaning campaign is scheduled to run from the 25th to the 31st of this month. The Municipal Health Bureau, together with the Municipal Public Security Bureau, will persuade shops and households to comply with the cleaning methods and implement the cleaning. Regarding factories, the Municipal Health Bureau will handle it together with the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. Regarding schools, the Municipal Health Bureau will hold cleaning lectures together with the Municipal Education Bureau, and the school authorities will order the students to assist their families in cleaning when they return home. The Municipal Health Bureau will be responsible for cleaning restaurants, shops, and various streets and alleys.

Garbage Disposal Methods 136

The Municipal Health Bureau believes that the street-side garbage cans set up in the past have had many drawbacks, so new methods have been formulated as follows: 1. All existing garbage cans within the area (i.e., within the jurisdiction of the Second District, Second Precinct, as follows) will be removed from the 15th of the 23rd year of the Republic. Each shop will be responsible for providing its own garbage can and dumping the garbage into the garbage truck at the specified times. 2. The garbage dumping times will be twice a day, the first time from 8:00 a.m. to 11:00 a.m., and the second time from 2:00 p.m. to 5:00 p.m. The street sweepers will notify the shops by ringing a bell. 3. The street sweepers should fulfill their responsibilities in collecting garbage. Shops are not allowed to give them any gratuities. If anyone extorts money, they can report it to the bureau for strict investigation. 4. The garbage can will be based on the house number, and the main household will be responsible for providing it for use by all families in the same house. Each house number must have at least one can. If there are many households in one house number, they must add more as appropriate. 5. The cost of preparing the garbage can will be borne by the head landlord. If the head landlord does not have a responsible person in Shanghai, the second landlord will pay for it first. If the second landlord is not in this place, the tenant will prepare it. The actual price will be deducted from the rent. The same applies when replacing it after it is damaged. If anyone refuses to acknowledge this, they can report it to the bureau for investigation. However, all residents should cherish the use of it and not deliberately damage it. 6. Residents along the road should immediately have someone take the garbage directly into the garbage truck after hearing the street sweeper ring the bell every day. Residents in the lanes should immediately dump the garbage into the truck as soon as the garbage truck enters the lane after hearing the bell. 7. All garbage cans must have a complete and tight-fitting lid. The style is as left (diagram omitted). 8. If any resident fails to prepare a garbage can within the time limit, they will be punished in accordance with the Administrative Execution Law.

Joint Public Notice by the Two Bureaus 137

A joint public notice by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Health Bureau states that although the matters of street cleaning and hygiene in this city have been reorganized several times, they have not yet achieved special effects. The reason is not entirely due to the lack of diligence in sweeping by the street sweepers and the insufficient application of garbage cans, but because citizens randomly dump garbage at any time and do not put garbage into the cans. Therefore, garbage cans are often seen empty, while the outside is littered with rubbish. Investigation and suppression are difficult to carry out thoroughly. In order to rectify the city appearance and prohibit vandalism, this bureau, etc., has submitted it to the municipal government for approval and decided to stop using the original public garbage cans within the jurisdiction of the Second Precinct of this Public Security Bureau from the 15th of January of the 23rd year of the Republic. Each shop must prepare a garbage can in the house, and the street sweepers of this Health Bureau will go to collect and transport it on time every day in order to avoid random dumping and maintain the cleanliness of the roads. All residents and shops within the area must prepare garbage cans as instructed before the 25th of this month. If they are not made after the deadline, this bureau, etc., will prepare them on their behalf and charge the price. In addition to making a sample of the garbage can and sending it to the Second Precinct of this Public Security Bureau for public viewing, the method is copied below and announced for general knowledge. This notice is issued by Wen Hongen, Director of the Public Security Bureau, and Li Ting'an, Director of the Health Bureau.
