Meeting Order 141

(1) Ring the bell to start the meeting, (2) Elect a temporary chairman, (3) Stand at attention with full ceremony, (4) Pay the highest respect to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Premier, (5) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will, (6) The chairman delivers the opening speech, (7) Report on the preparations, (8) Pass the constitution, (9) Elect executive economic committee members, (10) Discuss proposals, (A) Whether to install police bells and how to install them, (B) Advise various neighborhoods to reorganize or add fences, (C) Raise funds to run a crash course vocational training center for vagrants, (D) Whether to post moral persuasion slogans, (10) (1) The association's funding plan, (10) (2) Temporary motions.

Constitution Passed 142

Guan Gong was publicly elected as chairman to open the meeting according to the procedure. First, the chairman reported on the preparations and passed the constitution. Article 1 (Name): This association is jointly organized by people from all walks of life in the police, regiment, gentry and business circles in Shanghai South, and is named the Shanghai South Winter Defense Joint Committee. Article 2 (Purpose): The purpose of this association is to carry out the following types of association affairs during the winter defense period: (1) Proposing and assisting the police regiment in carrying out necessary measures for defense affairs, (2) Planning safety facilities for citizens, (3) Collecting citizens' opinions on theft prevention, (4) Deliberating on the resettlement of vagrants, (5) Handling moral persuasion and propaganda matters. Article 3 (Committee Members): There is no fixed number of committee members in this association. The district chiefs, precinct chiefs, detective team leaders, water patrol team leaders of the Public Security Bureau in the Shanghai South area, the commander, deputy commander, and team leaders of each team of the Shanghai South District Home Guard are ex officio committee members. Committee members of the Shanghai South Fire Brigade, directors of each district, committee members of charitable organizations, and representatives of various commercial organizations are ex officio committee members. Local enthusiastic gentry can become committee members of this association with the introduction of two committee members and the approval of this meeting. Article 4 (Organization): This association will have a number of economic committee members. All those who have not served as executive committee members will be elected as economic committee members to form an economic committee dedicated to planning the association's funding matters. There will be 35 executive committee members to form an executive committee. In addition to mutually electing 11 standing committee members to handle daily affairs, they will be in charge of the following groups of matters: (1) General Affairs Group, (2) Finance Group, (3) Document Group, (4) Design Group, (5) Investigation Group, (6) Public Relations Group, (7) Moral Persuasion Group, (8) Defense Group. Each group will have a director and a deputy director. The detailed rules for each group will be formulated by the groups themselves and submitted to the executive committee for approval. Article 5 (Meetings): The plenary committee will be held once a month on the 20th, and the executive committee will be held once a week on Saturdays. If necessary, it can be convened temporarily by the standing committee. At each meeting, one standing committee member will be elected, and the chairman will make a resolution with the attendance of one-third of the total members and the consent of more than half of those present. When the executive committee is in session, economic committee members may also attend and speak. Regarding matters of each group, a group meeting may be held to decide to report to the executive committee for execution. Article 6 (Funding): The association's funding is divided into two types: (1) Regular expenses are donated by various organizations that sponsor the association, (2) Business expenses are decided by the plenary committee, and temporary fundraising receipts and expenditures will be reported in detail after the end of winter defense. Article 7 (Detailed Rules): The detailed rules for the association will be formulated separately. Article 8 (Supplementary Provisions): These regulations shall be passed by the plenary committee and submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Government Garrison Headquarters for filing and implementation. The amendment procedures are the same.

Large Quantities of Foreign Flour Shipped to Shanghai 147

Foreign Merchants Suffer Losses Due to New Taxes

Chinese Factories Will Be Affected by Dumping

A large amount of American wheat flour has been shipped to Shanghai this year. Before the 10th of this month, various foreign merchants, upon hearing that the Jianghai Customs would add ten new taxes on New Year's Day next year, and that foreign flour imports would also be subject to tariffs, the flour merchants sent telegrams to the United States one after another, instructing them to ship large quantities of wheat flour to Shanghai as much as possible before December 31. Some of them had not yet been sold to the consignee, and they were also ordered to ship them out in advance for storage in Shanghai for successive sales in order to avoid paying import tariffs. After these telegrams were sent, American wheat flour was rushed to be shipped by rented ships at the beginning of this month. According to people in the shipping company in this city that loaded the American flour, there were hundreds of thousands of bags already en route. The first batch will be imported on the 23rd and 24th of this month. Unexpectedly, the Customs' new tax on foreign wheat and wheat flour was promulgated and implemented on the 16th, half a month earlier than the foreign merchants knew. This has made it difficult for various foreign merchants to advance or retreat regarding the huge amount of wheat flour that has already been shipped. If it is returned to the country, the shipping costs will be too high and the losses will be even greater. If it is shipped to Shanghai, the payment of new taxes will also require two or three hundred thousand yuan. It was reliably learned yesterday that it has been agreed to allow this batch of foreign flour en route to be shipped, and they will have to reluctantly pay the tax. In these ten days, huge amounts of foreign flour worth about one million yuan have been imported into Shanghai.

The Labor Dispute at the Two Railway Factories Was Not Resolved Yesterday 148

All the workers at the Wusong and Zhanghuabang Railway factories went on strike due to the expulsion of the head of the General Affairs Department, Mo Heng. The details were recorded in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday was the third day of the strike. All the workers still entered the factory at the usual working time, and dispersed to go home at 4:00 p.m., but they did not work in the factory and implemented a strike system. The order was still good. The craftsmen either read newspapers in the factory or chatted in the factory gate trade union. It is said that the strike seemed to be caused by the transfer of Cao Wenkui, a clerk in the Material Department, but in fact, after Director Mo concurrently served as the Director of Materials, the low quality of various materials purchased was unbearable for use. The workers resented the fact that the materials could not be used for work, which was a major reason for the strike. It was also said that when Sun Xuexiu, the former Director of Materials, was in office, he had to submit the samples and prices of the materials to the General Affairs Department for approval before they could be used. Now, the general affairs materials are all under the jurisdiction of Mo Heng. The situation in this regard can be clearly understood by discerning people. Yesterday, the Party Headquarters of the Two Railways, fearing that the situation would escalate, specially appointed Zhang Yunhe, the director of the Organization Section, Min Luoding, the standing director, and Cai Jinghai, a standing member, to come to Song after 3:00 p.m. They convened a meeting of all the workers in the factory gate trade union to give speeches, mostly advising the workers to wait for the Party Headquarters to meet with the superiors to resolve the matter. It was not until 4:00 p.m. that they dispersed.

It is also reported that, in view of the serious situation of the strike wave of workers at the Wusong machine factory on both routes, the Railway Bureau invited representatives from the Party Headquarters and the trade union yesterday (the 21st) to discuss a proper solution. It was decided to first form an investigation committee to thoroughly investigate the points of attack on Mo Heng. The candidates for the committee are Yuan Boyang, Wang Bi, Fan Shouzhi, Lu Baogao, and Pu Dengqing from the Bureau, Zou Kexin, Chen Chengshi, Li Dasan, and Xie Chengyu from the Party Headquarters of the Two Railways, and Min Luoding and Chen Bohua from the trade union. It is now scheduled for the above-mentioned 11-member committee to go to Wusong at 8:00 a.m. this morning to persuade the workers to resume work first, and at the same time, immediately start investigating the charges against Mo Heng, and complete the investigation within two weeks. During the thorough investigation period, Mo Heng will be suspended from his duties.

Page 9

Installing Wireless Radio Alarms on Cars 150

Contract Signed with the Municipal Council

Installation to Begin in February Next Year

According to the Central News Agency, the economy in this city has been declining in recent years, and there are many unemployed, which has led to desperate acts by restless elements. Robberies and kidnappings occur from time to time. The Public Concession Municipal Council has signed a contract with the Radio Protection Company to install wireless radio alarms on cars to provide security protection for citizens and increase the protection power of the police stations. The contract has been signed and installation has begun. According to a Central News Agency reporter, the details are as follows:

Contract Contents 151

The Radio Protection Company is managed by Mr. Li, a Chinese. Because kidnappings occur frequently in the Concession, the company requested the Public Concession Municipal Council in September to sign a contract to install wireless radio alarms and must grant it a three-year patent. After repeated discussions, the contract was signed on the 14th of this month. The main points of the contract are: (1) The Municipal Council allows the company to install wireless radio alarm radios in the designated police stations within three years. All installation costs will be borne by the company. (2) The Municipal Council is not responsible for compensation for future damages, etc. (3) The Municipal Council allows the police stations to immediately dispatch for rescue after receiving alarm reports, but the Municipal Council is not responsible if good results cannot be obtained. In addition, when alarm users install this type of wireless radio alarm with the company, they must sign a contract and pay a deposit of 25 yuan. If an alarm user falsely reports after installation, they will be fined 25 yuan each time. If there are three false reports, their alarm will be confiscated. (4) The Municipal Council and the Radio Protection Company both have the right to refuse alarm users to install this type of alarm. (5) If the company violates the provisions of this contract, the Municipal Council may suspend its business, but must notify it six months in advance.

Alarm Effectiveness 152

This type of alarm is specially installed on cars and is shaped like an electric bell installed on a door. When a car equipped with this type of alarm suddenly encounters bandits on the road, it can press the bell once, and the police station's radio will receive a very detailed alarm, including (1) where the car is, (2) the color and license plate number of the car, (3) the owner of the car, etc., all of which can be clearly known. After receiving the report, the police station will send out police officers to search for and capture the bandits. The method of use is extremely simple. The installation price of this type of alarm is 1,500 yuan per unit, and 200 yuan per year for the second year and below.

Installation to Begin 153

After the contract was signed, the Radio Protection Company installed wireless radios in the police stations. It is expected to be fully completed by the end of January next year, so the company has scheduled to begin installing alarm users' alarms on February 1 next year. The installation location of the alarm is inside the front of the car, while the bell-pressing mechanism can be installed next to any seat. After this device is implemented, those who ride in cars can be much safer, it is said.

Western Newspaper Reports 154

The Continental Daily News reports that a group of Chinese businessmen in this city have established a Wireless Protection Company. In September, the Shanghai Municipal Council granted the company a three-year exclusive license to operate a wireless alarm service in the International Settlement. A detailed contract was subsequently signed on December 13. The company is now actively preparing to commence operations in February of next year. According to the license and contract granted by the Shanghai Municipal Council, the company will provide and maintain wireless receiving sets for all police stations, at the company's expense. These receiving sets will work in conjunction with automatic wireless transmitters installed in private automobiles. Whenever a vehicle equipped with such a transmitter encounters danger, such as being accosted by bandits, a simple press of a button will transmit an alarm to all police stations, indicating the vehicle's location, type, and other necessary details. The police can then quickly rush to the scene to provide assistance. The company expects to complete all preparations by the end of January next year, and will begin accepting subscribers in early February. It is said that each subscriber will be required to pay an installation fee of approximately 1,500 yuan, as well as an annual maintenance fee of several hundred yuan, although the first year's fee is excluded. This ingenious device was invented by a European who wishes to remain anonymous. After contacting several Chinese businessmen, he arranged for them to invest in and establish the Wireless Protection Company. Although New York City also uses wireless alarm systems, the system to be implemented in Shanghai is different and far more sophisticated. When the company initially applied to the Shanghai Municipal Council for an exclusive license, the council ordered a trial to demonstrate its effectiveness. Chief Inspector E.W. Everson and other senior police officers supervised multiple trials, all of which were deemed satisfactory. Mr. Everson then formally applied to the Shanghai Municipal Council for the company to be granted an exclusive license. It is said that several police officers, including those in the Chief Inspector's intelligence division, are currently receiving training on how to operate these wireless receivers, which will be installed in all police stations. If the current number of personnel is insufficient, additional personnel will be assigned, at the company's expense. The company will maintain absolute confidentiality regarding its subscribers, so that bandits intercepting vehicles will be unaware that the police are about to arrive. It is also said that the company will soon apply to the Shanghai Municipal Government and the French Municipal Council for permission to operate this service exclusively within their jurisdictions. This will allow vehicles equipped with this device to travel anywhere in Shanghai without fear of danger.

Xu Yongzuo Improves Chinese Bookkeeping 155

More Than Thirty Types of Improved Account Formats

Successful Trials by Various Organizations, Companies, and Businesses

Chinese bookkeeping, as it exists today, can be broadly divided into two schools: Chinese and Western. Western bookkeeping uses horizontal registration, and the paper, ink, and writing instruments are all imported. The principles and methods of accounting are rigidly adhered to Western practices, making imitation not only difficult but also costly. Chinese bookkeeping uses vertical recording, and the paper, ink, and writing instruments are all domestic products. The principles and methods of accounting are familiar to the Chinese people, but the system is poor and lacks organization, resulting in chaos and confusion that undermine the fundamental principles of accounting. As a result, it is often criticized. Mr. Xu Yongzuo, an accountant in this city, has compiled more than thirty types of improved Chinese accounting books and forms based on more than ten years of research. Each type comes with detailed instructions, and a separate book, "An Introduction to Improved Chinese Bookkeeping," provides an overall explanation of the entire improvement plan. It has now been handed over to Standard Accounting Form and Document Manufacturing Co. for high-quality printing on domestic paper and is available for public sale. In this year of promoting domestic goods, this great work of organizing national essence and promoting domestic goods is particularly worthy of social attention. A reporter from the New Sound Society has made a special effort to investigate and record the details as follows:

Improvement Process 156

Between 1918 and 1919, the Shanghai Bank Weekly opened a special column for accounting research, publicly studying the science of accounting and bookkeeping. At that time, the newspaper was edited by Mr. Xu. Mr. Xu then became familiar with the accountant's business. He had more contact with Chinese bookkeeping and studied it in detail. In 1927, the China Economics Society invited him to give a lecture at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce. The topic of the lecture was "Improving Chinese Accounting Problems." At that time, Jinan University and Shanghai Business College also invited him to give lectures, forming a movement to improve Chinese bookkeeping. In 1928, the former Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Agriculture and Commerce advocated improving bookkeeping and specially appointed Mr. Xu as a member of the committee. In the same year, the Shanghai Institute of Certified Public Accountants, at the request of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, established a special committee to improve bookkeeping, and Mr. Xu was elected as a member. When the former Bureau of Industry and Commerce convened the National Industry and Commerce Conference, Mr. Xu participated in the event. In 1929, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce issued a letter inviting Mr. Xu to take charge of planning the improvement of bookkeeping. At that time, there was no consensus on whether to promote Western bookkeeping or abandon Chinese bookkeeping, so there were no concrete measures. In the past four or five years, Mr. Xu has been entrusted by major companies, firms, and organizations to plan bookkeeping organizations. For those who have been using Chinese bookkeeping, Mr. Xu has formulated improved Chinese bookkeeping methods. Since the trial implementation, the results have been remarkable. Even large-scale businesses have found it convenient to implement. In order to popularize the improvement of bookkeeping in China, Mr. Xu has recently spent half a year, based on China's inherent system and taking into account the latest theories in the world, using the most economical and practical methods, to compile a systematic and organized plan for improving Chinese bookkeeping, stipulating more than thirty types of account book and form formats, and compiling and publishing a book called "An Introduction to Improved Chinese Bookkeeping."

Trial Results 157

Over the past four or five years, Mr. Xu has formulated improved Chinese bookkeeping organizations for major companies, firms, and organizations. It is said that about fifty companies have effectively implemented them, such as Wuzhou Pharmacy, Sino-British Pharmacy, Jicheng Pharmacy, Taihe Pharmacy, Nanyang Tobacco Company, Huacheng Tobacco Company, Zhongnan Tobacco Company, Zhonghe Tobacco Company, Zhonghua Book Company, World Book Company, Datong Book Company, Shanghai Inland Tap Water Company, Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Bus Company, Star Film Company, Central Film Company, Star Grand Theater, Far East Public Sports Ground, Tianyi Printing Company, Sanyi Printing Company, China Commercial Savings Bank, Renjihe Insurance Company, Huaan Insurance Company, Huacheng Insurance Company, Samsung Cotton and Iron Factory, Hua Textile Dyeing Factory, Jiu Ji Timber Company, Dafeng Textile Company, Taishan Brick and Tile Company, Yizhong Fuji Porcelain Company, Guohua Coal Ball Company, China Match Company, Taikang Food Company, Chengmao Food Company, Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Joint Association of Machine-Made Domestic Goods Factories, Siming Guildhall, Xinwei Relief Society, Pushan Villa, Zhabei Charity Group, Xin Puyu Hall, Weizhong Shantang Lianyi Shanhui, Shangxian Hall, Women and Children's Hospital, Silk and Satin Trade Association Hangzhou Silk Group, etc.

Improved Features 158

According to accountant Xu Yongzuo, who spoke to a reporter from the New Sound Society, the ten major features of improved Chinese bookkeeping are: (1) Old-style Chinese account books only have two columns, upper and lower, with amounts, reasons, and notes all recorded in one place, making it inconvenient to record and even more difficult to check accounts. Improved Chinese account books are all printed with a fixed format. A certain grid records the reason, a certain grid records the amount, a certain grid records the date, and a certain grid records the page number, all clearly divided, so recording and reviewing are very convenient. (2) Old-style Chinese account books have never had a fixed registration method. How should our account books be registered? There is no standard, and the bookkeeper has complete freedom. Improved Chinese account books have detailed instructions printed on the last page of each account book, explaining the nature and usage of each account book. The bookkeeper can follow these instructions. (3) Old-style Chinese bookkeeping procedures have never been fixed, resulting in numerous errors and loopholes. In improved Chinese account books, the last page of each account book should have thirty-two bookkeeping rules for bookkeepers to follow. All procedures regarding opening accounts, recording accounts, posting accounts, and closing accounts are strictly regulated. (4) In Chinese customs, personnel in charge of account books generally do not indicate their names in the account books. When there are discrepancies or errors, they often push the blame onto each other, making it difficult to hold them accountable afterward. Improved account books have a list of personnel in charge printed on the first page. First, the name of the account book, the name of the person in charge, and the date of acceptance should be filled in one by one, and then bookkeeping can begin. The same applies when handing over the account book, so the responsibilities of the bookkeepers are clearly defined. (5) Our old-style account books are not paginated, so pages are often missing or torn out. This is a source of fraud for bookkeepers. Improved Chinese account books stipulate that account books are divided into three types: fifty pages, one hundred pages, and one hundred and fifty pages. The number of pages is pre-determined, which not only prevents fraud but also allows each other to indicate the page numbers when posting accounts, making it easier to review. (6) Our old-style account books only have two types: running ledgers, which do not have borders, and meal ledgers, which have borders. This is too simple and cannot be applied to various industries. The formats of improved Chinese account books, including application forms, total more than thirty types, most of which are available for various industries. (7) Old-style Chinese businesses have never had so-called forms, which is a major flaw in accounting organization. It should be known that forms have evidentiary effect, reconciliation function, and overview function in bookkeeping, which are indispensable. Improved Chinese and Western account books have seven important forms. All commonly used forms are complete. (8) Leaving aside the difficulty of obtaining Western bookkeeping talent, the fact that paper, ink, and writing instruments must be imported, resulting in high prices and heavy expenses, is already too uneconomical. The materials used in improved Chinese and Western account books are all domestic products, and the binding and printing are both exquisite. Compared with Western account books, there is a meaning of promoting domestic goods, and compared with old-style account books, there is the advantage of high-quality materials. (9) Accounting is ultimately not something that can directly generate profits, so the accounting department should strive for cost savings. Every time Western bookkeeping is adopted, if the scale is slightly larger, several thousand yuan must be spent on account books and forms every year, which is too wasteful. Improved Chinese account books have beautiful materials and low prices. Not only are they cheaper than Western account books, but they are also more economical than old-style account books. (10) The organization of improved Chinese bookkeeping account books, the classification of accounts, and the nature and usage of their various contents are all explained in detail in "An Introduction to Improved Chinese Bookkeeping." All new and old bookkeeping personnel can understand it after browsing. If there is anything unclear, you can consult the Xu Accountant Firm at No. 38 Edward Road, Shanghai.

Assassination of Tang Jiapeng Case 159

Rebuttal Argument Concluded

The Sentence Must Be Pronounced Again

Tang Jiapeng, the former manager of the Great World entertainment venue, was shot and killed by assassins in front of the Great World at 2:00 a.m. on June 18 of this year. A passerby, Wu Guangcai, was also killed by stray bullets. After the incident, detectives from the French police special agency successively arrested the criminals Zhang Tinggui (alias Xiao Sizi), a native of Funing, and Zhao Guangfu, a native of Yangzhou. A White Langlin pistol used by Zhao to kill Tang was recovered. They were handed over to the Second Special District Local Court and prosecuted for premeditated murder. After several court hearings and interrogations, the police verified that three of the eight bullet casings found at the scene matched Zhao's pistol. The defendants also confessed that they were entrusted by Wang Jinkui, who is still at large, to collude with Zhou Ershuishui, a carpenter who is also at large, to carry out the shooting. The trial had been declared concluded, and the sentencing was originally scheduled for the day before yesterday, as reported in the previous newspaper. The presiding judge, Wu Fanglian, has now reviewed the entire case and determined that it is still necessary to investigate whether the four bullets extracted by doctors from the body of the deceased, Tang Jiapeng, in the hospital were fired from the pistol in question. Therefore, on the day before yesterday, Judge Wu went to the First Criminal Court and ordered the two defendants, Zhang and Zhao, to be brought before the court. He announced the cancellation of the conclusion of the rebuttal argument, briefly interrogated the two defendants, and ordered that the rebuttal argument be reopened on the 29th of the month.

Zhang Yaonan Conspires with His Lover to Bring His Sister to Shanghai for Sale 160

The World Actually Has Such Absurd Things

Zhang Shunsheng, a native of Yixing, is already sixty-eight years old. He used to work as a tax collector in the local county government, but he has recently retired due to old age. His son, Zhang Yaonan (alias Chen Peigen), is twenty-eight years old and cannot inherit his father's career. He is dedicated to wandering and is especially fond of women. He formed an inextricable relationship with Yan Hongbao, a young woman from the same village. Yan is only twenty-two years old and has a stunning appearance, which makes Yaonan even more infatuated. Last month, he listened to Yan's instigation and took his twelve-year-old younger sister, Zhang Shunmei, from his hometown to Wuxi, intending to sell her. They stayed in Wuxi for a long time, but no one inquired. So they took Yan and her sister and took Shunmei from Wuxi to Shanghai by military transport. Along the way, he ordered Shunmei to call Hongbao "mother" to disguise their true relationship. As expected, they did not reveal any flaws. After arriving in Shanghai, Yaonan returned to his hometown alone, and handed Shunmei over to Hongbao for her to dispose of freely. Hongbao solicited in many directions, and finally sold her a few days ago to Jiang Ximei, an eighteen-year-old young woman living at No. 24 Daqing Lane, Nanjing Road, for 210 yuan. At that time, Ximei also thought that Hongbao and Shunmei were mother and daughter. Only after the transaction was completed did she realize that there were never mothers and daughters who were only ten years apart in age. She became very suspicious and repeatedly questioned Shunmei, only to learn the truth. Fearing that concealing the truth would cause trouble in the future, she immediately tried to notify the girl's father, Zhang Shunsheng, to come to Shanghai to resolve the matter. However, the old man was unfamiliar with the place and had no way to find them after arriving. Later, he asked his clansman, Zhang Shouqing, to help him find them. Yesterday, father and daughter were reunited. He wanted to take her home immediately, but Jiang Ximei demanded 300 yuan in compensation, otherwise she would not return the girl. The old man argued with her, and during the conflict, the matter was reported to the Old Zhabei Police Station. After investigating, the police arrested Yan Hongbao for kidnapping. Her sister and Zhang Yaonan had already left Shanghai and could not be arrested. Yesterday, the police escorted Yan to the First Special District Local Court, where Judge Feng Shide interrogated her. The police representative, lawyer Zhang Shizhu, explained the case. Later, Jiang Ximei also hired lawyer Fan Gang to the court to file an incidental civil suit against the defendant to recover the purchase price. After careful interrogation by Judge Feng, Yan Hongbao was sentenced to one year in prison. The girl was taken away by Zhang Shunquan. Jiang Ximei's request for compensation for the purchase price should be filed in a separate lawsuit.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Notifies All Trade Associations to Comply with the Regulations and Re-elect 165

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce notified all trade associations yesterday, saying, "Dear Sirs, on the 20th of this month, we received Order No. 17241 from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, which stated, 'We have received Order No. 7454 from the Municipal Government, which stated, "We have approved Advisory Letter No. 20910 from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, which stated, "All chambers of commerce and industrial and commercial trade associations in various places should comply with Article 19 of the Chamber of Commerce Law, which states, 'The term of office of executive and supervisory committee members is four years, with half of them being re-elected every two years, and they may not be re-elected consecutively.'" It has been found that most of those who have re-elected in accordance with the law and submitted their names for record have done so, but there are also those who have not completed the re-election matters upon the expiration of the two-year term and have submitted them to the Ministry for review, which is unavoidable. According to Article 19 of the Implementing Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law, "When a reorganization or re-election is due, the current officers shall be responsible for handling it. If it cannot be completed by the deadline, they shall not continue to exercise their powers." Therefore, groups whose re-election is due should not be negligent, lest they harm themselves. If the public association and the chamber of commerce are both due for re-election, the election of the public association should be held before the election of the chamber of commerce in order to comply with the procedures and avoid disputes. In addition to the separate consultations, we are hereby consulting for your information and instructing you to comply," etc. With this approval, we are hereby ordering your association to comply and instruct all industrial and commercial trade associations to comply accordingly," etc. We have received the order and are sending it to you for your information and compliance."

Pudong Electric Company Connects Zhabei Current 168

Electricity Will Be Supplied Starting Today

The Pudong Electric Company, in order to supply electricity economically during the transition period, in addition to its own installed capacity of 600 kilowatts, also purchased 2,000 kilowatts of electricity from the Chinese Electric Company to supplement it. Fearing that the electricity supply was limited and insufficient for development, it signed a contract with the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company in February of this year to purchase an annually increasing amount of 500 kilowatts of electricity to be transferred to the three districts of Gaoqiao, Gaohang, and Luxing, as well as the northern part of the Yangjing district. All wiring projects have been actively prepared for over half a year and have been gradually completed. Electricity will be supplied starting today. The details of the various projects are as follows:

Building a Distribution Substation 169

In January of this year, the company purchased two mu, five fen, eight li, and three hao of land along the Pu River in Taojiazhai, Gaohang District. Because the terrain was low-lying, it hired workers to fill the land with mud to bring it level with the levee and built wooden fences around it to prevent tidal erosion. A two-story distribution room was built. The upper floor is equipped with receiving and distribution equipment, and the lower floor is equipped with cables. Four worker dormitories were also built next to the room, which were gradually completed in October of this year.

Burying the Under-River Cables 170

The location of the cables crossing the river is of utmost importance. After repeated surveys, it was decided to be on the Pudong bank of the Wuchuan Road North Jun Gong Road East in Zhabei, (about 1,130 meters south of the Qiu River Port). First, a submarine cable was buried to cross the Huangpu River to the company's distribution substation in Pudong. In July of this year, an order was placed with the British firm Kai Nengda for a 920-meter-long submarine cable with three steel cores, a cross-sectional area of 125 square millimeters, oil paper insulation, lead pipe wrapping, and double steel strip armor. In July of this year, an order was placed with the British firm Kai Nengda for a submarine cable 920 meters in length with three steel cores, a cross-sectional area of 125 square millimeters, oil paper insulation, lead pipe wrapping, and double steel strip armor. In order to protect the cables, Chinese "Cable Crossing, No Anchoring" warnings were posted on each bank of the river. One warning sign was placed on each bank of the river cable crossing. The signs were lit at night, and a joint notice was issued by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Shanghai Municipal Utility Bureau. The Jianghai Customs Port Authority also issued a notice strictly prohibiting all vessels from anchoring in the area to avoid damaging the cables and hindering the power supply.

Installing Distribution Equipment 171

The distribution room is divided into nine compartments with reinforced concrete partition walls. Three compartments are equipped with power receiving equipment, and six compartments are equipped with power distribution equipment. All meters and oil switches are installed by Huatong Electrical Machinery Factory. After testing, they are in good condition.

Installing Power Lines 172

According to the original plan, the power output lines from the electrical room are divided into north and south lines, reserving space for three lines to prepare for future expansion in the distribution room. Six reinforced concrete power poles are erected on the east side, using angle iron as the frame, to install the underground cable junction boxes and lightning arresters on them, connecting to the north and south main power lines. The north main line extends from Gaoqiao Port to Jiangxinsha, and the Gaoqiao Town south line extends to Donggou Town, connecting to the newly installed pole lines recently set up on Pudong Road. After electrification today, it will first supply the Jiangxinsha and Gaoqiao Town areas. Within three months, it will be gradually extended to Donggou, Yangjing, Qichangzhan, Lujiazhai, Lannidu, and other places, switching to the Zhabei power source. In the future, the company will have ample reserves and reliable power supply, and the prospects for business are indeed promising.

Those with minor damage have already received compensation.

It is planned to increase the speed to 13 nautical miles per hour, so that Shanghai to Qingdao will only take one day, which will surely be welcomed by passengers. At the same time, three wharf boats of Jinfusheng and Jie Jinfashe parked there were also damaged. Later, the company sent personnel to inspect and confirmed the facts. It has agreed to compensate for the damaged boats and has paid compensation to the two boats that were slightly damaged. The remaining damage to the wharf dolphins, etc., is still under negotiation.

Cooperation between the Cotton Textile and Yarn Industry

The overall situation is in the front, and we will go all out to make cotton weaving factories use domestic yarn as much as possible, so that our country's textile industry will not be oppressed by the dumping policy of Japanese imperialism and be on the verge of bankruptcy. Cotton weaving factories can use pure domestic raw materials to create finished products, providing the country's people with the supplies they need, leaving a glimmer of hope for the national economy, and turning misfortune into good fortune. Furthermore, we will urge the improvement of textile factory products and the improvement of economic organization, so that the economic relationship with cotton weaving factories is harmonious and close, and we will struggle with Japanese imperialism in the economic market. The reporter inquired at the Navy Headquarters yesterday and learned that at about 2:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, Zheng Tici, the captain of the Qingyun ship, and He Tianyu, the captain of the Hai'ou ship, visited Chen Jiliang, the commander of the First Fleet, and reported the escape process. It is now known that the two men are still staying on the two ships and have not gone to Beijing to report the news to Minister Chen Shaokuan.

Woman Chen Ying Arrested 182

丨For Participating in Reactionary Work丨

The supervisors of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau’s Supervision Office learned the other day that a Guangxi woman named Chen Ying, age 22, who resides in the pavilion room of a certain lane and number on Xipushilu Road in the French Concession and previously studied at Jinan University and China Public School, has recently been participating in the Communist Party’s reactionary work and has been appointed as a member of the bogus Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee. She has been active in Shanghai, conducting secret propaganda, and so on. The supervisors immediately reported this to Director Wen Hongen, prepared a document, and went to the political department of the French police station to report and request assistance in arresting and extraditing her for trial. The director of the department approved the request and immediately ordered Chinese and Western detectives to rush to the address, arrest Ms. Chen, and search a large number of communist books and leaflets in the room, bring them back to the police station for detention, and send them to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court for trial yesterday afternoon. Judge Guo, along with the Fan and Sun magistrates, jointly opened the Third Criminal Court with Chief Prosecutor Zhao to conduct the trial. Attorney Yao Zhaodi appeared in court on behalf of the police station, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau also sent personnel to the court with a document to request the transfer of the defendant. The court announced that because the case involved politics, public attendance was prohibited. According to the results of the trial, the police station opposed the transfer because the defendant resided in the concession and committed the crime in the concession, which should be under the jurisdiction of the concession court. The prosecutor also expressed agreement. The police station's reason for filing the case was that it was under the jurisdiction of this court for trial. Finally, the court announced that the defendant need not be transferred and would be detained pending a scheduled trial.

Precious Jewels Such as Pearls, Platinum, Jade, and Emeralds Can Be Authenticated with Ultraviolet Light 183

New Contribution from the Zhenru Forensic Institute

Anyone Can Send Items for Authentication

According to Lin Jiyun, director of the Zhenru Forensic Institute of the Ministry of Justice Administration, the institute recently tested the ability to use ultraviolet analyzers to authenticate the authenticity of precious items such as pearls, gemstones, platinum, jade, and emeralds. If so, it will provide great convenience to jewelers, pawnshops, and modern wealthy ladies. Those who treasure or buy and sell treasures can send them to the institute for authentication at any time for the sake of prudence. It is reported that the institute, in addition to accepting civil and criminal cases sent by the court, is also willing to accept entrusted inspection events from groups or individuals.

He developed a sense of world-weariness. At about 11:30 a.m. yesterday, he committed suicide by swallowing a sedative potion. He was discovered by someone and was rushed to Renji Hospital by Bao Tan of No. 227 in a car. The treatment was ineffective, and he died at 6:55 p.m.

Female Thief Appears in Robbery Late at Night 189

A Qín Teacher Suffers Robbery Halfway

The Female Thief's Face Shows Signs of Smoking

Chen Nianzhi, residing at No. 110 Guangxi Road, who is a qín teacher, was accompanied by his friends Geng Dalin and Jin Changsheng at 2:40 a.m. on the 16th of this month, and when they arrived at the intersection of Yunnan Road and Hankou Road, they were suddenly encountered by three robbers, two men and one woman, each wielding a pistol, blocking their way. They were forbidden to make a sound, and Chen's woolen hat, overcoat, and shorts, worth a total of 32 yuan, were robbed and the robbers fled. Chen reported the information to the police station, stating the faces and clothing of each thief, and stating that the female thief had signs of smoking on her face. The police chief, upon receiving the report, ordered Chinese detectives Zhao Fuhai, Cui Chengke, and others to cooperate with Chen Nianzhi and the two witnesses Geng and Jin to go to various public places and tea rooms to secretly investigate. At about 4:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, they suddenly saw a woman with a face full of smoke coming out of a certain alley in Guangxi Road. After careful observation by the witness, they recognized her as the female thief who was robbing on the spot at the time, so they arrested her along with a suspect, Yan Hongmu from Shaoxing, and took them to the Xinzha Police Station. Upon questioning, the female thief's name was Qian Xuezhen, 23 years old, a local. She was ordered to be detained. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the First Special District Court. According to the case stated by Wang Yaotang, the lawyer of the police station, Qian Xuezhen was charged with robbery under Article 348 of the Criminal Law, and it was requested that the suspect Yan Hongmu be detained for investigation. In addition, the victim Chen Nianzhi and witnesses Geng Dalin and Jin Changsheng submitted a case to prove the robbery situation and pointed out the face of the defendant Qian Yunzhen. Although her ability to determine was not accurate, her figure, hair, etc. were all very similar to the female thief who was robbing. Upon questioning, Qian Yunzhen refused to admit it. Judge Xue ordered Qian and Hong to be returned to custody separately, and to be re-questioned at a later date after the investigation.

Property Owners Urgently Request the Public Works Department to Order the Company to Open Water 190

The Real Estate Association Advises Digging Artesian Wells for Relief

After the British-owned Shanghai Water Company closed the main water pipe in Tonghaili, Tongzhou Road, Hongkou the other day, more than two thousand residents were greatly panicked. The other day, the Shanghai Water Company of Huaideli, Qipulu, also sent Chinese and foreign dignitaries to the neighborhood to shut off the water pipes, causing the tenants in the neighborhood to question the owners, Tao Rangji, and the clamor did not stop. The owners of the neighborhood went to the Real Estate Association yesterday, asking it to forward the request to the Public Works Department, ordering the Water Company to open the water immediately to resume drinking water. The neighborhood immediately forwarded the request to the Public Works Department for investigation.

Tao Rangji's Letter Tao Rangji sent a letter to the Real Estate Association yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir, the Shanghai Water Company's water bills for our property at No. 3 to No. 19, Lane 384, Huaideli, Qipulu have not been issued for four months. We do not know the water price and they have not come to collect the bills. This morning, the company suddenly closed the water meter, and the tenants came to question us one after another, and the clamor did not stop. According to this situation, the company is unknowingly making a mistake by cutting off drinking water, which violates people's livelihood and concerns people's lives. When we reasoned with them, the Chinese and foreign personnel evaded us in every possible way. We hereby send this letter to your association, asking it to forward it to the Public Works Department and quickly order the Water Company to open the water immediately to resume the lives of the people. Respectfully, to the Real Estate Association."

Letter to the Public Works Department (1) Dear Sir, according to a letter from our association member Ji Ji (see above), they came to the association, and we should send a letter to your bureau for strict investigation, so as to give importance to people's lives. Respectfully, to the Director-General of the Public Concession Public Works Department. (2) Dear Sir, according to a letter from our association member Kaigeng Ji Renting Accounting House, the Shanghai Water Company often forces the landlord to pay the water bill for his identity, otherwise they will cut off the water and not allow him to use it. However, we have found that the tenants owe rent for two or three months. The landlord has not received the rent, so how can he advance the water bill? This kind of coercion is beyond reason. We hope that your association will find a way to deal with this. Respectfully, to the Director-General of the Public Concession Public Works Department. (3) Dear Sir, according to a letter from our association member, the Real Estate Department of Shanghai China Reclamation Bank (see previous report), Shanghai Water Company still intends to illegally cut off water, putting users to death, even though the water fee committee has been established, which shows that they are completely insincere and extremely rude. According to the situation in the letter, we should send a letter to your bureau immediately, ordering the company to open the water in order to maintain people's lives and avoid embarrassing the justice authorities. Respectfully, to the Director-General of the Public Concession Public Works Department.

Reply to the Reclamation Bank The Real Estate Association replied to the Real Estate Department of the Reclamation Bank yesterday, saying: "Dear Sir, we have respectfully received your letter of December 19 regarding the illegal water outage by the Shanghai Water Company and know everything. In addition to going to the Public Concession Public Works Department to order the Water Company to open the water and wait for a solution, we are corresponding to inform you and hope that you will immediately drill an artesian well to seek a permanent solution and reduce the living burden of users. Respectfully, to the Real Estate Department of the Reclamation Bank."

###檀香桂元業聲請各界援助

The Sandalwood and Dried Longan Industry Requests Assistance from All Sectors

工部局非法徴收食物捐

The Municipal Council Illegally Levies Food Donations

上海市檀香桂圓號業同業公會、爲反對公共租界工部局非法徴收食物捐、請求各界援、昨特發通函云、逕啟者、敝會員榮春等十三號聯名函稱、茲緣敝號等開設於福建路、查牌子最老者已有五十餘載、次亦十餘年矣、（有帳册及房捐票爲憑）歷來未聞有與熟食物店同須捐領執照之例、惟民國十六年十一月及二十一年七月間、公共租界工部局衛生處、曾有向敝號欲徴收食物捐之舉、均經請求納稅華人會據理力爭、及法院主持公道、乃得免除、皆有舊案可稽、按十六年十一月二十五日第一特區法院違警庭沈推事審理本案時、曾云、工部局所訴榮春永春等號違章不適用洋涇浜章程第三十四條、如欲令該號領照者、須將洋涇浜章程重行修訂、方有依據、沈推事主持公道、保障華商權利、其功德實堪歌頌、查工部局一再朦訴、迄今六年、審理不下數十庭、敝號一再抗爭否認該捐稅、不屈不撓之精神、努力奮鬥、深恐影響國家及租界全體華商之權利前途、殊非淺鮮、而關係敝業者實甚經微、每號一季不過費　元耳　今年工部局衛生處、又向第一特區法院、爲訴敝號等於四月十日六月二十三日七月二十八日十一月三十日、在福建路開設食物店、未向該衛生處捐領執照、指爲違章、顯與事實不符、因敝號等所售各物、多係檀香·及桂圓等生乾果·他如胡桃·茘子·蓮子·等物、實與衛生無礙、查洋涇浜章程第三十四條、載明茶館飯店酒樓跳舞場書場等須領執照、卽工部局中國食物出售店執照、其解釋此照對於一切售賣鮮魚鮮肉家禽蔬菜及「熱食店、」皆得應用、觀此更可明瞭敝號等根本非「熱食店、」亦非「食物店、」所謂「熟食店、」係指顧客在客飲食、非購出者、卽根據其英文解釋（Ｅating　house）食物店、這個（Ｅailng）就是（正在吃）意思、（Ｅating　hosue）就是到食物店裏吃、則敝號等所售之貨、與「食物店」及「熟食店」根本不同該衛生處所訴違章、顯無根據　似此苛捐擾商、非法壓迫、斷難承認、且値此商業蕭條之際、豈堪任其誅求、肆意宰割、永無止境、若不團結力爭、吾弱小商人、將無噍類矣、又本月十五日第一特區法院鄧推事審理本案時、不加審察洋涇浜章程第三十四條之規定、遽行諭令處罰十元、幷須補捐實屬藐視商民、擅判罰捐、殊羅甘服、故請邵繩祖·湯天陶·律師·依法聲請法院正式審判外、爲特函請貴會准予擴大宣傳、並請求各界援助、俾達撤銷苛捐之目的等情前來、准此、查右述各節、確係實情、相應函請各界各團體、本愛國之熱心、予以援、一致力爭、俾達撤銷苛捐之目的、以維華商一線之生計、不勝感　之至云、

The Shanghai Sandalwood and Dried Longan Trade Association, in opposition to the illegal food donation levied by the Public Concession Municipal Council, requests assistance from all sectors and issued a special circular yesterday, which states: "To Whom It May Concern, Our members, Rongchun and thirteen other firms, jointly wrote a letter stating that our firms are located on Fujian Road. The oldest of our businesses has been established for over fifty years, and the others for more than ten years (with account books and house tax receipts as proof). We have never heard of any precedent where businesses like ours, selling dried goods, are required to donate for and obtain a license as with cooked food stores. However, in November of the 16th year of the Republic of China (1927) and July of the 21st year (1932), the Public Concession Municipal Council Health Department attempted to levy food donations from our firms. On both occasions, the Chinese Ratepayers Association reasoned with them and the court upheld justice, thus exempting us. There is an old case on file to prove this. According to the ruling by Judge Shen of the Violation Court of the First Special District Court on November 25, 1927, the Public Concession's claim that Rongchun, Yongchun, and other firms violated regulations does not apply to Article 34 of the Yangjingbang Regulations. If the Council wishes to require these firms to obtain a license, it must revise the Yangjingbang Regulations. Judge Shen upheld justice and protected the rights of Chinese merchants, a deed worthy of praise. It is noted that the Municipal Council has repeatedly brought frivolous lawsuits over the past six years, resulting in dozens of court hearings. Our firms have repeatedly resisted and denied the donations. Our indomitable spirit and diligent struggle, fearing that it would affect the rights and future of the nation and all Chinese merchants in the concession, is not insignificant. The amount involved for our industry is extremely small, costing each firm no more than a few yuan per season. This year, the Municipal Council Health Department has once again sued our firms in the First Special District Court, claiming that we opened food stores on Fujian Road on April 10, June 23, July 28, and November 30 without obtaining a license from the Health Department, which is inconsistent with the facts. The items sold by our firms are mostly sandalwood and dried longan, dried fruits, such as walnuts, lychees, and lotus seeds, which are harmless to health. Article 34 of the Yangjingbang Regulations clearly states that tea houses, restaurants, dance halls, and story houses must obtain licenses, namely the Municipal Council's Chinese Food Sales Shop License, which is interpreted as applying to all sales of fresh fish, fresh meat, poultry, vegetables, and "hot food stores." From this, it is clear that our firms are fundamentally not "hot food stores" or "food stores." The so-called "cooked food stores" refer to places where customers eat on the premises, not those who buy food to take away, which is based on the English interpretation (Eating house). 'Eating' means 'eating,' and 'Eating house' means eating at the food store. Therefore, the goods sold by our firms are fundamentally different from 'food stores' and 'cooked food stores.' The Health Department's accusation of violation has no basis. Such harsh donations disturb businesses and are an illegal oppression. It is difficult to accept, especially during this time of commercial depression. How can we tolerate their extortion, arbitrary slaughter, and endless demands? If we do not unite and fight for our rights, we small merchants will face extinction. Moreover, on the 15th of this month, Judge Deng of the First Special District Court, without carefully examining the provisions of Article 34 of the Yangjingbang Regulations, hastily ordered a fine of ten yuan and demanded back payments, which is a contempt for merchants and an arbitrary penalty. We are unwilling to accept this. Therefore, we have retained lawyers Shao Shengzu and Tang Tiantao to formally petition the court for a trial, and we have issued a special letter to your association requesting permission to expand publicity and requesting assistance from all sectors to achieve the goal of abolishing this harsh donation. Upon consideration of the above, the facts are indeed true. We hereby request all sectors and organizations to show patriotic enthusiasm and provide assistance to strive together to achieve the goal of abolishing this harsh donation, to maintain a lifeline for Chinese merchants. We would be extremely grateful."

Cause of the Fire

Xu Lianke, head of the Lawa District Security Corps, has lived for generations at No. 2, 99th Street, Xujiahui West Town. The house has five bays, with front and rear buildings and four side rooms, and is an old-style bungalow. Xu has four brothers: the eldest, Lianjia, lives in the eastern section of the front building; the second is Lianke, who lives in the eastern section of the rear building; the third brother is deceased; and there is a sister-in-law, Xu Lu, who lives in the western section of the rear building. The fourth, Lianji, lives in the western section of the front building and has already moved out. Xu Lu has one son and one daughter. Her son, named Fugen, is twelve years old and currently studying. Her daughter, named Zixin, is twenty-two years old. The mother and daughter both work as factory workers at the Great China Overshoe Factory. The remaining two rooms in the west side room are rented to two tenant families from Nanqiao, Jiang Hongchun and Hu Yunting. Yesterday morning, around 7:00 AM, Xu Lu and her daughter went to work at the factory, leaving only Jiang Wu, the wife of tenant Jiang Hongchun, at home. Around 9:30 AM, Wu was careless while cooking, and the remaining firewood in front of the stove caught fire instantly. By the time Xu Lu heard about it and returned home, the fire had already broken through the roof. Unfortunately, the fire was raging, and it was impossible to control it. Although firefighters from various fire brigades and the chiefs and police officers of the Second Sub-Bureau of the Sixth District arrived to put out the fire, there was no tap water installation in the area, and the river behind was blocked with silt, making the efforts futile. The fire was finally extinguished at 11:15 AM.

總計損失 193

Total Losses

計焚去後棣及東西廂房共九間、前棣五間、西半已被敲毁、内中以徐陸氏受害最重、焚去鈔洋五百元、及伊女自新之妝奩、無一餘存、故總計損失當在萬元以上、

A total of nine rooms in the rear building and east and west side rooms were burned down. The western half of the five rooms in the front building were also destroyed. Among them, Xu Lu suffered the most damage, with 500 yuan in banknotes and her daughter Zixin's dowry burned, with nothing remaining. Therefore, the total loss is estimated to be over 10,000 yuan.

工部局將徴收春季總捐 195

The Municipal Council Will Levy the Spring General Donation

工部局一九三四年春季之市政總捐、將於一月一日到期、除華式房屋、仍派員收取外、所有西式房屋、居戶於接到通知後、應卽將捐欵送交江西路二零九號捐務股核收、

The Municipal Council's 1934 Spring Municipal General Donation will expire on January 1st. Except for Chinese-style houses, which will still be collected by personnel, all Western-style houses' residents should submit the donation to the Donation Department at No. 209 Jiangxi Road after receiving a notice.

又捐務股車捐徴收組、自一月三日起、至十七日止、每日辦公、自上午八點半起、至下午五點半止、中午亦不休息、以期納捐人便於繳納、凡汽車·脚踏車·自用人力車·公用人力車·小車·手車·之執照、均由此組辦理、

The Vehicle Donation Collection Team of the Donation Department will work daily from January 3rd to the 17th, from 8:30 AM to 5:30 PM, without a lunch break, to facilitate payment by donors. Licenses for automobiles, bicycles, private rickshaws, public rickshaws, small carts, and handcarts will all be handled by this team.

又售賣外國酒品（不在店内飲用者）之分等及捐額、自一月一日起、照議决案略有訂正、已由工部局在公報内公布、

The classifications and donation amounts for the sale of foreign alcoholic beverages (not for consumption on the premises) have been slightly revised according to the resolution, effective from January 1st, and have been announced by the Municipal Council in the Gazette.

182nd Time

The 182nd inspection report of the Central Bank's issuance reserve states: "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the issuance of convertible banknotes by this bank. The 182nd inspection was conducted on December 20th of the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933) at the Issuance Bureau of this bank. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible banknotes issued is 69,373,616 yuan in silver. This includes 63,435,100 yuan in silver dollar banknotes and 5,938,516 yuan in subsidiary coin banknotes. The total amount of reserve funds for convertible banknotes is 69,373,616 yuan. This includes a cash reserve of 56,583,616 yuan in silver dollars. This cash reserve includes 52,296,634 yuan stored in the bank's issuance vault, 1,485,266 yuan stored in branch banks in various ports, and 1,800,716 yuan deposited with other banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 12,790,000 yuan in silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible banknotes issued is 416,715.40 yuan. The total amount of reserve funds for customs gold convertible banknotes is 416,715.40 yuan. This reserve includes 6,995 taels, 3 mace, and 9 fen of gold, calculated at a fixed price of 5957, equivalent to 416,715.40 yuan in customs gold. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%.

City News 206

▲ Taihe Pharmacy's Winter Medicines. The Taihe Pharmacy on Fourth Avenue has a wide variety of seasonal winter medicines. Tonics include Ren Zhong Bao, Bai Bu Wan, and cod liver oil. Cough medicines include Bao Fei Jiang and Bao Fei Yi. Cosmetics include Mei Mei Cream and Xiang Mi. Supplies include hot water bottles and foot warmers. Each product has proven to be effective. Customers are enthusiastically buying them. Recently, due to the sudden cold, there has been an increase in frostbite sufferers. The pharmacy's unruptured frostbite medicine can be applied to red and swollen frostbite to dissipate and heal it. For ruptured frostbite, the pharmacy's ruptured frostbite ointment or 606 ointment can be applied to close the wound and heal it.

▲ Three Major Companies Vigorously Promote Victory Brand Sai Xiu Paste. Since the introduction of Victory Brand Sai Xiu Paste, it has gained considerable authority in the field of women's new clothing. It is also used for gifts, with various landscape and floral designs drawn with the paste. However, some unscrupulous merchants, driven by greed, are counterfeiting inferior goods to deceive the market. Dahua Trading Company (Victory Brand Chun Xiu Paste General Management Office) at No. 617, 6th Floor, Continental Emporium, issued a solemn warning to correct the public's perception. The three major companies on Nanjing Road all recognize the paste as a new invention for women's new clothing and are vigorously promoting it. New New Company recently announced to the public that during the New Year's sale period, anyone who purchases five yuan or more of Victory Brand Sai Xiu Paste at the company will receive a set of exquisite 1934 calendars as a souvenir.

▲ Yu Le Guo Grand Opening Imminent. The newly established Yu Le Guo goldfish garden has commenced with arrangements since raising enough capital. The garden is located on Haig Road in Western Shanghai. All work on fences, buildings, well digging, tank installation, pond excavation, etc. has been completed one by one. Various precious goldfish have also been moved to the garden for rearing. The retail department at the Continental Emporium is currently being renovated internally. It is expected to have a formal opening around January 4th, simultaneously with the garden. It is heard the retail department will have three large rooms, holding a goldfish exhibition on the opening day for tourists to enjoy, and Mr. Wu Jiren will compile a special book on goldfish rearing to be distributed to all.

▲ Folies Ballroom Hires Famous South American Band. The magnificent Folies Ballroom at No. 9 Route Doumer in the French Concession opened at the beginning of the month. Its splendid appearance and exquisite interior have already caused a sensation throughout Shanghai. The ballroom's beautiful dancers, melodious music, clean Western food, and comfortable seating are all considered top-notch. The ballroom is warm as spring, making it the best in Shanghai. Starting on the 20th, the ballroom is bringing in a famous South American band to perform various famous songs. At the same time, more than ten artists from Beiping (including Mr. Pan Delin) will perform various unimaginable stunts.

▲ Sino-French Pharmacy Beef Juice and Chicken Broth Sell Well. The Sino-French Pharmacy on Beijing Road in this city is holding a month-long sale from the 17th of this month. In addition to selling all medicines at special low prices, it also has sacrificial products to treat customers. On the first day of the sale, the buy-one-get-one-free offer on Double Lion Brand beef juice and chicken broth resulted in the sale of over 5,000 bottles in the main store and its branches. These beef juice and chicken broth products are made using the latest cold maceration method of nutritional chemistry, preserving all the nutrients and proteins. Therefore, they are rich in substance, delicious in taste, and particularly effective. At this time of heavy frost and severe cold, they are truly the first holy medicine among tonics.

▲ Zhonghua Shoes on Nanjing Road is Selling Shoes at a Discount and Giving Away Tickets. Incoming Correspondence 209

The Overview and Future Development Plan of the China National Aviation Corporation in 1933 by Dai Enji

The China National Aviation Corporation, a joint venture between China and the United States, has been operating for over three years. With the guidance of the government, the support of people from all walks of life, and the efforts of the company's colleagues, the past achievements have been praised by the public. At the beginning of this year, Enji was ordered to take charge of the company. I worked day and night, not daring to slack off, and I was particularly dedicated to the work of the three major routes. The Shanghai-Beiping route was opened on January 10 this year, the Chongqing-Chengdu route was opened on November 11 this year, and the Shanghai-Guangdong route was opened on October 24 this year. From then on, the north, south, east, and west are connected, which is convenient for Chinese and foreign people. The Chongqing-Chengdu route is particularly convenient. In the past, it took ten days to travel between Chengdu and Chongqing by both land and water. Since November 11 this year, the plane can travel more than a thousand miles in two hours, and there is no longer the feeling of the difficulty of the Shu Road.

The company, in view of the prosperity of commerce and the development of passenger and mail services between Shanghai, Hankou, Chongqing, and Chengdu, plans to use the latest type of aircraft for flights in the summer of next year. This type of aircraft is stable and comfortable, and its cruising speed is 150 miles (about 450 li), which is one-third faster than the current aircraft. In this way, it can leave Shanghai in the morning and arrive in Hankou at noon, and all mail can be delivered in the afternoon. Leaving Hankou the next morning, it can also arrive in Chengdu at noon on the same day. Therefore, the journey between Shanghai and Chengdu is only two days, and the journey in the air is only ten hours.

The history and achievements of the China National Aviation Corporation have long been known to the public. It is praised as a giant of commercial aviation in our country. All future plans will be realized as scheduled. The following is a list of statistics from January to the end of November 1933:

Number of passengers carried from January to the end of November 1933: 2,349

Passenger miles accumulated from January to the end of November 1933: 819,693

Mail carried from January to the end of November 1933 (in kilograms): 40,767

Flight miles from January to the end of November 1933: 571,912

From the above observations, our country's commercial aviation has a potential for rapid development in the future. For the needs of rapid development, the China National Aviation Corporation must train talents as a necessary plan. All kinds of equipment needed for development must be urgently worked on, so as not to become a deformed development. Therefore, new types of manufacturing are also pursued within the possible range to achieve the goal of self-sufficiency.

When the company first started, it hired many foreign personnel. Now, our country's personnel are competent. For example, the radio department is entirely composed of our country's personnel. Our country's personnel are also responsible for dismantling and repairing aircraft, and the effect is remarkable. The existence period of the Sino-American contract is only ten years, and it has been three and a half years. The time of six and a half years will arrive in a blink of an eye. Therefore, the cultivation of talents cannot be delayed, because it will be used in the future. The equipment of Longhua Airport has gradually changed. It was originally planned to build two runways for the takeoff and landing of aircraft. One of them has already been completed. Our country's airfield has never had a runway before. This is actually a pioneer. The second one has also started construction and should be completed by the end of this year. A new shed will be built next spring to make it complete. When it first opened, some passengers may have imagined the simplicity of the airport. Comparing the past and the present, it is no different from heaven and earth.

Furthermore, currently, China National Aviation Corporation only has domestic flights and only carries domestic mail. It is expected that it will soon be able to carry international mail as well. This is what the company is looking forward to day and night.

Ministry of Education to Separately Issue Various Regulations on Mass Education 211

It is heard that regulations on mass schools, mass education centers, libraries, and other items have been drafted and will be discussed and decided at a meeting of the Mass Education Committee to be convened in January next year before being promulgated for implementation.

Ministry of Education Orders Colleges and Universities to Form Graduation Examination Committees 212

▲ List of Committee Members Should Be Submitted to the Ministry First

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to all public and private universities and education departments of provinces and cities to instruct colleges and universities to comply with the law in forming graduation examination committees, saying, "Article 17 of the University Regulations stipulates that graduation examinations shall be conducted by committees organized by professors, associate professors, and outside experts from the school, with the president of the school as the chairman. Each subject's examination must have an outside committee member participating within the possible scope. Article 17 of the College Regulations also has the same provision. However, since the promulgation, the implementation of various schools has varied. In order to emphasize this, it is specially re-ordered that from this academic year, the graduation examinations of various schools shall be handled in accordance with the above regulations, and a list of committee members shall be prepared in advance and submitted to the Ministry for approval to comply with the law."

Second Guangdong Provincial Education Association 214

▲ Held in Guangzhou on the 1st of This Month

(Guangzhou News) The Second General Assembly of Members of the Guangdong Provincial Education Association was held in Guangzhou on the 1st of this month. Forty-seven representatives from education associations in various counties and cities registered. Representatives from various institutions and organizations were sent to observe the ceremony. At 9:00 AM, the opening ceremony was held in the conference hall of the Education Department of the Provincial Education Association. Jin Zenceng, Su Binglin, and Zeng Jinghan were publicly elected as the presidium. Jin Zenceng delivered the opening speech, stating that the association is holding its second general assembly of members today in accordance with the association's charter to re-elect directors and supervisors. Currently, there are more than 50 representatives from various counties and cities, which is enough to meet the legal quorum. When the first congress was held, it coincided with the Japanese invasion of the Northeast. To date, national revenge has not been avenged, and a year has passed in a blink of an eye. External humiliation is becoming more urgent, and internal troubles are deepening. The national pulse is in danger. Our colleagues in the education community are responsible for the rise and fall of the country. How should we earnestly do salvation work? The province's three-year administrative plan has now been implemented in order. How should we understand and implement it to complete the entire plan? Today, we gather here with all of you. Everyone should express their opinions and contribute to the authorities. The proposals of this congress will comprehensively address current needs and propose six important proposals. I hope that everyone will discuss them at length. After the resolution is made, I hope that you will follow the implementation so that you will not fail to convene this congress. After the speech, the secretary of the Provincial Education Association reported on the general situation of the association's affairs, saying that the association's affairs are divided into the following items: 1. Publication, 2. Research, 3. Lectures, 4. Exhibition, 5. Competition, 6. Renovation, 7. Miscellaneous Affairs, 8. Abstract of the Resolutions of the Board of Directors and the Board of Supervisors, 9. Field Work. Regarding the first item, publication, there are the association's magazine, a general overview of the Guangdong Provincial Education Association, a compilation of observation notes from the Northeast war zone, Guangdong teachers, recent physiological science, and a general overview of vitamins. Regarding the second item, research, there are anti-poison speeches, diplomatic speeches, and the compilation of practice character scale. Regarding lectures, a national language lecture hall was held. Regarding exhibitions, a book exhibition on Sino-Japanese issues, an education supplies exhibition, a secondary school painting exhibition, and a primary and secondary school students' practical handicraft exhibition were held. Regarding competitions, an anti-Japanese essay competition, the third one-act play competition for secondary school students, and the three primary and secondary school students' practice character competition were held. Regarding renovations, the association's wall was rebuilt, Jiuyao Pond was renovated, and the library's partition was changed. Regarding miscellaneous affairs, the area of ​​this area was measured, the rules and times of the association's sports ground were set, the Guangzhou Exhibition was attended, school fields were re-approved, school fields were surveyed, a new conference hall was planned, and the association's office was planned to be rebuilt. Regarding the board of directors, 16 meetings have been held, and the board of supervisors has held three meetings. Regarding field work, members have been sent to participate in a total of 62 meetings of various mass organizations. After the report, representatives from various organizations, such as Xie Yingzhou, gave speeches. The meeting was adjourned at 11:50 AM. In the afternoon at 2:00 PM, the congress convened to review the various proposals. At 4:30 PM, the representatives of the education associations of various counties and cities went to Huanghuagang to pay tribute to the 72 martyrs. In the evening, the director of education, Xie Yingzhou, held a banquet to entertain. On the morning of the 2nd, the congress continued to meet to discuss the proposals, and the closing ceremony was held on the afternoon of the 3rd.

Anhui Education Department Orders Provincial Middle Schools to Improve Six Points 217

The Anhui Education Department previously sent members to inspect various provincial secondary schools. The Education Department, based on the inspection report, yesterday ordered the schools to earnestly improve the following six points: (1) The cleanliness and hygiene of the school are closely related to the health of the students. From now on, all schools should pay close attention to this facility. The dining hall, kitchen, bathroom, toilet, and sewer, which are most prone to dirt, must be cleaned and swept frequently. (2) In order to train students to work, the cleaning and sweeping of classrooms, self-study rooms, and dormitories should be assigned to the students. The instructors should supervise and assess them at any time. (3) All teachers and students in the school must wear uniforms of the same length to invigorate the spirit and rectify the appearance of the school. (4) The doors of the student dormitories must be locked at all times except during the designated time. No one is allowed to enter without permission. (5) Students' clothing, books, and all kinds of miscellaneous items should be placed in a fixed place and arranged neatly. (6) Daily morning exercises or inter-class exercises are beneficial to the body. They must be earnestly supervised and carried out. Absences are not allowed without excuse.
