Film Special

A Visit with the Owner of Jincheng Theater 308

— Yun Yan

Everyone keeps shouting that the film industry is in a slump, but new theaters are still being built one after another. Now, on the corner opposite the Beijing Grand Theater, a tall building has been built. The skeleton of the building is almost complete, and it looks quite magnificent. In the high sky in front of the gate, a white sign with black characters reading "Jincheng Grand Theater" is revealed before my eyes. "Oh! Jincheng Grand Theater, so it's here!" I thought to myself, and then looked at the small characters below the large characters "Jincheng Grand Theater." Only then did I know that their office was opposite. Thinking that it was still early, I might as well go and talk to the staff inside, maybe I could get some new news about this theater that is about to open.

No sooner said than done, I stepped into their office. A young man with a slender figure and a lively spirit came out to greet me. It turned out that he was the owner of the theater, Mr. Liu Zhongliang. I told him my name and purpose, and we sat down on a long sofa and began to talk.

I first asked Mr. Liu if the Jincheng Grand Theater was a company or not; if there were any foreign shareholders; and how much capital it had. Mr. Liu told me that their company was built by him and his brother Zhonghao, who put up the capital. There were no other shareholders, and there was no question of foreign capital. As for the capital, their budget was 500,000 yuan.

When I heard that two brothers had put up so much money to build a movie theater, I couldn't help but admire their courage and boldness. Because most of the movie theaters in Shanghai are companies. Just as I was about to continue asking questions, I suddenly saw Mr. Zhonghao walking over with a large bundle of seat cover materials, such as silk and velvet. Mr. Zhongliang also introduced me to him. Because he had to go inside to discuss other matters, he asked Mr. Zhonghao to talk to me instead.

"Do your brothers have a lot of experience with movies?" I continued to ask.

Mr. Zhonghao smiled and replied, "We founded a World Grand Theater in Nanjing, and it's been four years now. It's been pretty good. Last year, we bought a piece of land near the World Grand Theater and wanted to build a larger Guotai Grand Theater. Later, because we saw that many of the big movie theaters in Shanghai were funded by foreign capital, and the profits were flowing out, it was really disheartening. Therefore, my brother and I made a grand wish to create a popular theater in Shanghai. The current Jincheng is the realization of our plan."

"Then how many seats does your theater have? How will the ticket prices be in the future?"

Mr. Liu replied, "There are 1,800 seats. As for the ticket prices, they haven't been determined yet. In short, we are determined to promote film culture and popularize mass entertainment. Although the theater is built like an aristocratic place, the ticket prices will never be aristocratic."

"Will your theater show domestic films or foreign films in the future?"

"This matter has not yet reached the stage of announcement, so please excuse me for not being able to tell you. However, whether it's Chinese or foreign films, we are very strict about film selection."

We also talked about the importance of sound equipment. When Mr. Jin heard this, he said excitedly, "Although we have tested several sound systems, we have not yet made a decision. We are probably going to use the latest 1933 R.C.A. giant machine. Not only that, but for the comfort of the audience, we have also installed the latest air conditioners and heaters."

At this point, someone inside asked him to answer the phone, so I excused myself and left.

Film Review

Review of "Tiger Shark" 309

— Ling He

To suit the needs of the audience, films must be stimulating and lighthearted. This is a trend that can be seen in current American films and will inevitably become popular.

Take "Tiger Shark," produced by First National Pictures, for example. In addition to the essential love story, it also features the excitement of man fighting shark and the lightness of witty dialogue. It combines both stimulation and relaxation.

With the ocean as its backdrop, the film presents the lives of seaside fishermen, their fishing methods, the scenery of the ocean, and pure love in a vivid and lovely way, which cannot help but evoke our infinite admiration. Although this is not a documentary, the incorporation of a story and the insertion of ample local color are ultimately the greatest features of this film. This is where the value of the film lies.

Regarding the depiction of the protagonist, Mark, we must believe that the author was indeed successful. Loyalty, straightforwardness, and courage are merely simple literary adjectives, but to express them in a film, it is necessary to make us feel and understand them through the visuals. This is a very difficult task. The screenwriter allows him to fully display his lovable personality in his friendships. He sacrifices himself for his friends and saves poor orphans. However, although he needs the warmth of the opposite sex, women will not love him. Only an exceptional girl who repays his kindness is willing to reluctantly marry him. Of course, such a union is easily shaken for a passionate young man, just like a couple with a large age gap. When she meets the friend of her vigorous and strong husband, she quickly loses faith in her husband. In this regard, we cannot blame her in any way. At the same time, Mark's friend, who is like a brother, lives with the conflicting emotions of love and friendship, which also makes people feel sympathy for him. And the protagonist's temporary punishment of his good friend out of jealousy is not an excessive act. Everyone is a complex character, and everyone is tormented by conflicting emotions. As such, the screenwriter's ability to depict such conflicts and contradictions so perfectly is truly very successful. Similarly, the director's meticulous and economical depiction of love, as well as his strong emphasis on sketching life, is also a great success. Of course, minor shortcomings or methodological errors are inevitable. For example, the portrayal of the woman is too inadequate, which is a flaw. In addition, he also pays attention to sound effects, such as the monotonous piano music on a moonlit night, the sound of gunfire when lovers embrace, and the sound of bells when Mark is dying, all of which are not exaggerated and are very harmonious with the plot. Although these are all old methods.

Lead actor Edward G. Robinson, after "Little Caesar" or "Two Seconds," now has "Tiger Shark," which truly makes us believe in his high level of acting skills. Admittedly, his personality is consistently tough and bold, but it is greatly different in terms of good and evil from "Little Caesar" and quite similar to "Two Seconds." His performance alone is already very commendable. Lee Shumway has no special achievements, and the female lead is even more superficial. The cinematography is very successful.

"Stark Nature" 310

— Moore

Stark Nature

Human concepts are extremely complex. Therefore, "Tarzan the Ape Man" and the like satisfy a novelty and stimulation, and at the same time, they are an escape from reality and a pursuit of primitive life. Therefore, old film critics still have to make various embellished justifications for this point, but a film like "Stark Nature" leaves no room for justification.

What unfolds before the audience is the scenery of Africa; what is introduced to the audience are the foolish and docile natives. Moreover, here, we see Africa's abundant products and the endless reserves of gold and silver mines, which strongly hint at "Go to Africa!" Even if the lands of Africa have been divided up, there are still plenty of fat and blood to be squeezed from this unexploited group. Isn't it true that twentieth-century aggression does not necessarily require occupying land?

Moreover, it is not enough for the film to write these things from a positive perspective; it also finds material and spiritual justifications for the aggressors, namely, the white man's sense of superiority over all other races. In other words: it is the so-called civilizing mission of the white race. This point is written in the script as much as possible using contrast and setting off. Their intention is not only to say that invading Africa is helping the natives progress, but also that developing mines is like "discarding bad goods on the ground." Africa is the Africa of the white man. We have been hearing this phrase for more than a year. The survival of the fittest, the laws of natural selection, and Mr. Huxley's philosophy have a pro-Boer partiality. To those who say "philosophy is a partisan science, and so is the art," here, they encounter an iron-like answer!

Not only in terms of content, "Stark Nature" is a thorough propaganda film, but also in terms of form. Ordinary jungle films only introduce the protagonist's journey. At most, they mention the protagonist's return home, but "Stark Nature" is a narration after returning home. From this point, we already know that the author's intention is to propagandize.

As for the technical aspects, first, we must know that "Stark Nature" can be said to be a newsreel and a scenic film because there is no story in the middle. Therefore, there is nothing to say about the screenplay. However, the editing has some good points. Because it is a dancer's narration, he allows the audience to understand this point everywhere. The method is through "prompts," and these "prompts" are seamlessly integrated with the overall unfolding. For example, when the natives dance, they are followed by the dancers of the burlesque show, which are not only similar in some places but also used for comparison. At the same time, the dancer's narration is triggered by the scene, and when he sees this kind of "burlesque dance," he thinks of the natives dancing, which is similar to it. Or, for example, when he talks about the natives dancing and wants the listener to concretely know the dance posture, he points out the similar "burlesque" dance as an example, which is extremely clever.

Latest News from Tianyi 311

— Xi

▲A Movie Star: Filming of "A Movie Star" began in the summer, and nearly half a year has passed. Although it has been completed successfully, editing will still take time. This film uses a film company as its background. From the general manager to the laborers, everyone is shown on the screen. The scene of shooting a sound film is also introduced on the screen. Many people want to visit the film company's studio, but they often cannot find a way to enter. Now, in "A Movie Star," you can see it very clearly. The film is named "A Movie Star," but in reality, all the male and female stars participate in it. Therefore, there are more stars in "A Movie Star" than in any other film. With that being said, this film's title is a bit misleading.

▲Two-Year Plan: This two-year plan is not like the Soviet Union's "Five-Year Plan," which will only be completed after two years. These two "years" are the titles of two new films. One is "Passionate Youth," and the other is "Fleeting Years." They are directed by Tang Jie and Gao Lihong, who have newly transitioned from acting to directing at Tianyi. "Passionate Youth" stars Wang Yuanlong and Ye Qiuxin, and "Fleeting Years" stars Hu Shan and Ye Qiuxin. One is a patriotic drama, and the other is a moral drama. The themes of both are very good. These two films have been in production for more than two months, and now they have both been completed. The two-year plan can finally be declared complete.

▲Three Peking Operas: "Auspicious Land," directed by Shao Zuiweng and starring Chen Yumei, has now been sent to Beijing for review and will be released soon. Although the film is set in the countryside, there are many magnificent scenes in it. Just the scene of Xu Hongye marrying Xiang Gu, with hair ornaments, elegant clothing, and the clinking of cups, is already very lively. The three Peking operas are especially wonderful. The first opera is Miss Zhang Wenqi's "Farewell My Concubine," the second opera is Miss Fan's "Huai Du Pass," and the third opera is Zhang Zhenduo (as Xu Hongye) and Ye Qiuxin's (as Xu's concubine) "Mei Long Zhen." The two are singing enthusiastically on stage when suddenly a servant comes to report that the old master has died. Therefore, Xu Hongye does not have time to remove his makeup, takes off his beard, and hurriedly runs off the stage. For a moment, the order is in chaos, and the congratulatory guests become mourners.

▲All Sides Autumn Heart: Ye Qiuxin, the newly discovered star of the film world in 1933, her beauty can simply be a model for all beauty and is worthy of being called a "model beauty." She has recently been suddenly promoted to the leading role in four films, and the people co-starring with her are all first-class superstars in the film world, such as Chen Yumei in "Flame of Youth," Hu Shan in "Fleeting Years," Wang Yuanlong in "Passionate Youth," and Hu Shan and Lu Lixia in "A Movie Star." Like a thunderclap out of the blue, Qiuxin can also be very proud. A poem praises her: "Autumn heart is more beautiful than spring heart, all sides are exquisite, reflecting the superstars."

▲Five Routes of Advancement: Schools have some kind of three-three system. Now, Tianyi's film production can be said to be a five-five system. The films that have been completed but not yet released are: "Auspicious Land," "Flame of Youth," "Passionate Youth," "A Movie Star," and "Fleeting Years," a total of five films. There are also several films planned to be produced. One is "Happy Enemies," starring Chen Yumei, one is "Spring Dreams in the Dance Palace," starring Wang Cilong and Lu Lixia, one is "Roots Do Not Meet Before Marriage," starring Xue Juexian and Tang Xueqing, one is "Lin Chong," starring Wang Yuanlong, and there is also "Peace Blossom," originally written by Zhang Henshui and adapted by Yan Duhe, with the female lead played by Chen Yumei, and the rest of the cast is yet to be determined. With such five routes of advancement, it will surely create a dazzling, colorful spectacle that is even more beautiful than Zhuge Wuhou's Eight Trigrams Formation.

Movie Novel

Shanghai 24 Hours (2) 312

— Tianfu

(3) The Fate of Man and Dog

There is only one world, but the people living in this world are governed by an unknowable fate into two completely different circles. 丨丨 The day is gradually getting late. After the signal for the end of work at the yarn factory rang, the people in the factory poured out of the gate like a tide. 丨丨 Mr. Zhou, the comprador, was driven by a motorcycle to buy many expensive sweets to go back to his mansion to see his wife. 丨丨 At this time, his wife just happened to get up 丨丨 Hundreds and thousands of male and female workers dragged their tired bodies back to their shacks to rest. The injured child was also carried home by his sister and several workers.

The so-called "home": is a small mezzanine. Old Chen, who works as a vendor, is preparing to cook dinner. There is a commotion outside the door, and his injured brother is carried in. This unexpected misfortune hits Old Chen's heart like a punch. He is flustered and loses his composure. "What's going on? What's……?" He asks in a panic, and his sister tells him, crying, with the last sentence being: "The doctor said... he won't make it..."

Sadness, sorrow, and anger are concentrated in the minds of the two people at this time. Just let him die like this? At least get a doctor to take a look, of course. But what about the money? What is groped out of the pocket is only enough to eat pancakes! 丨丨 The two people look at each other with pitiful eyes. Finally: "You take good care of him. I'll go get some money from your sister-in-law." Old Chen says these words decisively and goes out.

Old Chen's woman works as a maid at Xie's mansion. 丨丨 Old Chen's sister and brother were able to go to work at that yarn factory thanks to their sister-in-law's introduction. 丨丨 He goes straight to Zhou's mansion. He gets five or six dollars from his woman, but he sees a sad scene at Zhou's mansion 丨丨 A veterinarian's bill collector is collecting a bill from the comprador's wife: the medical expenses for a pug cost thirty silver dollars.

"Look! Other people's dogs cost so much money to treat when they get sick!" Old Chen and Old Chen's woman look at the backs of the comprador's wife and the bill collector, silent, like two towering stone statues.

(4) The Lesson of the Rats

At seven o'clock, dusk quietly creeps into the embrace of this big city. With the money, Old Chen hires a doctor to examine his brother once. After the doctor leaves, looking at the child lying stiffly on the bed, he says sadly to himself: "Some people wear good clothes, eat good food, and play with good things; even dogs cost dozens of dollars to treat when they get sick. What about us?……"

Situation of Organization and Facilities of Yunfei Automobile Company

Self-Made Car Bodies 313

Yunfei Automobile Company puts special effort into the construction and style of car bodies. Therefore, the main work of the carpentry workshop in the head office is to engage in the construction of the car frame, which is the foundation of the car body. All car frames are made of especially strong, light, and absolutely non-decaying Philippine super-grade wood. This wood is always kept in large quantities to supply the manufacture of new car bodies. This is because, in order to meet the needs of business, new cars must often be added. The frames that are made, if they are of special dimensions, are all protected with a special metal containing copper to prevent rust. In addition to the car body frame, the screen frame is also manufactured and assembled by the carpentry workshop. If you visit and observe in person, you can see all kinds of car bodies in the process of being manufactured at a glance. This is not only for new cars, but also for vehicles that must have their bodies removed after ten months of driving and completely rebuilt.

Yunfei Main Office New Building on Great Western Road

Widespread Branch Stations 314

Yunfei has more than a dozen branch stations. They are all located in key areas and provide convenient services. In addition to the main station, the larger branch stations can accommodate more than fifty cars, which can definitely meet the needs of each location. Yunfei has many branch stations, so no matter where you are in the city, once you call for a car, the nearest station can immediately dispatch a car to go. As for after the ride is over, wherever you get off, the car will return to the station nearest to that location. This saves time and fuel, and the car will last longer. The allocation of vehicles to each station is determined based on need. This is based on the time of day and the weather.

Vehicle Inspection 315

Yunfei Automobile Company stipulates that each car wheel must enter the dock for inspection every ten days and be given various minor repairs. Every ten months, the car is completely disassembled and repaired separately. For example, the chassis is repaired by the chassis workshop, and the engine is repaired by the machine workshop, so that it is perfect and flawless, and no different from new. Other parts, such as crankshafts and transmissions, are all subjected to final inspection before being reassembled into a car. The various spare parts that are prepared are too numerous to count, such as springs and spark plugs, and are all neatly displayed for immediate replacement. Furthermore, all parts used in the car body, such as door locks, as well as various tools used in the machine workshop, are self-made and do not need to be sought externally. This shows the grand scale, complete equipment, and exquisite technology of the company. As for seeing the working situation at that time, one can deeply believe that Yunfei automobiles drive safely and quickly through the streets, which is undoubtedly after a great deal of heavy work.

Driver Training 316

Yunfei Company is extremely careful in selecting drivers. Therefore, its restrictions are very strict. The Yunfei Vehicle Affairs Office knows that the issue of driver training should be given extreme importance. Therefore, it often gathers drivers at the head office to teach them all the knowledge about their work, explaining repeatedly and in detail. Each gathering has about fifty or sixty people. The main purpose of the conference room set up in the Yunfei head office is for training drivers. As for the main points of the training, safety is of course the highest principle. Therefore, all necessary knowledge about machine parts, as well as traffic rules and first aid knowledge, are all emphasized. As for being familiar with the routes and treating customers kindly and respectfully, these are even more essential conditions for being a Yunfei driver. In short, safety and service are the two major principles that Yunfei diligently trains its drivers in.

Retrofitting Airplane Tires 317

The number of Yunfei vehicles that have been retrofitted with Goodyear aircraft tires has now reached more than eighty. Retrofitting with new tires costs the company a lot, but for the sake of customers, the benefits are not insignificant. These new tires have a particularly large surface area and are extremely strong and superior, which is sufficient to increase the safety and comfort of passengers. Goodyear aircraft tires are the culmination of many years of experience and are truly worthy of being a guarantee of safety and comfort. Yunfei is willing to make huge sacrifices and resolutely retrofit them, based on the spirit of service and entirely for the benefit of customers.

Renji Road Branch New Building 318

Yunfei's Employees 319

Fourteen years ago, Yunfei had twelve cars, only twelve drivers, and only nine internal staff members, totaling about twenty people. But as of today, fourteen years later, there are 56 accounting staff, 93 telephone operators, 165 copper painters, 43 car washers, and 305 drivers, totaling as many as 662 people. Compared to the past, it is like the difference between heaven and earth.

Passenger Statistics 320

The total number of Yunfei passengers this year is expected to exceed 4.5 million. According to historical statistics, Yunfei Company's business has increased by about 32.5 times in fifteen years. In other words, the number of passengers increases by more than double each year, and the increase has never been interrupted. Among them, the increase was especially large between 1930 and 1931.

Uniform Pricing 321

What is the displeasure of passengers if they have to haggle over prices or argue over fares when hiring a car? Yunfei Automobile's price is three yuan per hour, that is, one yuan every twenty minutes. It has been implemented consistently and remains unchanged. This is the regulated price in Shanghai. Under normal circumstances, this point is not worth mentioning. But in the event of a major incident, such as after the January 28th Incident, Yunfei Company alone still adhered to the regulated price, not avoiding difficulties and dangers, and doing its best to serve all sectors of society, and never taking the opportunity to exploit them. This is commendable and worthy of praise.
